  <script>
    // ===== 관리자 확인 =====
    const user = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_user') || 'null');
    if (!user || user.role !== 'admin') { window.location.href = '../index.html'; }

    // ===== 브라우저 기본 드래그앤드롭 차단 (파일 열기 방지) =====
    document.addEventListener('dragover', e => e.preventDefault());
    document.addEventListener('drop', e => e.preventDefault());

    // 드롭존 이벤트 바인딩
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const dz = document.getElementById('sopDropZone');
      if (dz) {
        dz.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); dz.style.borderColor='var(--primary)'; dz.style.background='rgba(79,70,229,0.05)'; });
        dz.addEventListener('dragleave', () => { dz.style.borderColor='var(--gray-300)'; dz.style.background='transparent'; });
        dz.addEventListener('drop', e => { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); dz.style.borderColor='var(--gray-300)'; dz.style.background='transparent'; handleSopDrop(e); });
      }
    });

    // ===== AI 설정 바인딩 =====
    // AI_CONFIG는 ai-provider.js에서 선언됨. 없으면 window에 폴백 생성
    if (typeof window.AI_CONFIG === 'undefined') {
      window.AI_CONFIG = { scriptProvider:'gemini', quizProvider:'gemini', chatProvider:'gemini', videoProvider:'none', keys:{ gemini:'', siliconflow:'' }, models:{ gemini:'gemini-2.5-flash', wan:'Wan-AI/Wan2.2-T2V-A14B' } };
    }

    // ===== Gemini API 공통 호출 (항상 서버 경유) =====
    window.callGemini = async function(prompt, options = {}) {
      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          prompt,
          model: options.model || 'gemini-2.5-flash',
          generationConfig: options.generationConfig || { temperature: options.temperature || 0.7, maxOutputTokens: options.maxOutputTokens || 2048 }
        })
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      return data?.text || data?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '';
    }

    // ===== 멀티 관리자 역할 시스템 =====
    const adminRole = user.adminRole || 'superadmin';
    const adminBranch = user.adminBranch || '';

    function hasPermission(action) {
      if (adminRole === 'superadmin') return true;
      const denied = ['sop_edit','sop_create','sop_delete','employee_all','learning_path','settings','chat_logs_all','reports_all','admin_manage'];
      return !denied.includes(action);
    }

    function getAdminList() {
      const defaults = [{ id:'demo-admin', name:'관리자', email:'admin@test.com', role:'superadmin', branch:'' }];
      return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_admin_list') || JSON.stringify(defaults));
    }
    function saveAdminList(list) { localStorage.setItem('sop_admin_list', JSON.stringify(list)); }

    (function ensureCurrentAdminInList() {
      const list = getAdminList();
      if (!list.find(a => a.email === user.email)) {
        list.push({ id:user.id, name:user.name, email:user.email, role:adminRole, branch:adminBranch });
        saveAdminList(list);
      }
    })();

    function getFilteredEmployees(allEmps) {
      if (adminRole === 'superadmin') return allEmps;
      return allEmps.filter(e => e.branch === adminBranch);
    }

    function getFilteredChatLogs(allLogs) {
      if (adminRole === 'superadmin') return allLogs;
      const myEmps = getFilteredEmployees(EmployeeStore.getAll());
      const myEmails = new Set(myEmps.map(e => e.email));
      const myNames = new Set(myEmps.map(e => e.name));
      return allLogs.filter(l => myEmails.has(l.email) || myNames.has(l.employeeName || l.userName));
    }

    function renderRoleBadge() {
      const el = document.getElementById('sidebarRoleBadge');
      if (!el) return;
      el.innerHTML = adminRole === 'superadmin'
        ? '<span class="role-badge superadmin">&#127775; 본사 관리자</span>'
        : '<span class="role-badge branch-manager">&#127978; 지점장: ' + adminBranch + '</span>';
    }

    function applySidebarPermissions() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.admin-sidebar nav a[data-require]').forEach(a => {
        if (!hasPermission(a.getAttribute('data-require'))) a.style.display = 'none';
      });
    }

    function applySopPagePermissions() {
      const el = document.querySelector('#sopListView .topbar-actions');
      if (el && !hasPermission('sop_create')) el.style.display = 'none';
    }

    function renderAdminManage() {
      if (!hasPermission('admin_manage')) return;
      const list = getAdminList();
      const c = document.getElementById('adminListContainer');
      if (!c) return;
      c.innerHTML = list.map(a => {
        const sa = a.role === 'superadmin';
        const rb = sa ? '<span class="role-badge superadmin">본사 관리자</span>' : '<span class="role-badge branch-manager">지점장: '+(a.branch||'미지정')+'</span>';
        const ab = !sa ? '<button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:4px 12px;font-size:12px;color:var(--danger);border-color:var(--danger);" onclick="demoteAdmin(\''+a.email.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\')">권한 해제</button>' : '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-400);">-</span>';
        return '<div class="admin-card"><div class="admin-avatar">'+(a.name||'?').charAt(0)+'</div><div class="admin-info"><h4>'+(a.name||'-')+'</h4><p>'+a.email+(a.branch?' / '+a.branch:'')+'</p></div>'+rb+' '+ab+'</div>';
      }).join('');
    }

    function openAddBranchManagerModal() {
      const emps = EmployeeStore.getAll();
      const adminEmails = new Set(getAdminList().map(a => a.email));
      const cands = emps.filter(e => !adminEmails.has(e.email));
      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      m.innerHTML = '<h3>지점장 추가</h3><p style="font-size:14px;color:var(--gray-500);margin-bottom:16px;">기존 직원을 지점장으로 승격합니다</p>'+
        '<div class="form-group"><label>직원 선택</label><select id="bmCandidateSelect">'+(cands.length>0?cands.map(e=>'<option value="'+e.email+'">'+e.name+' ('+e.email+') - '+e.branch+'</option>').join(''):'<option disabled>승격 가능한 직원이 없습니다</option>')+'</select></div>'+
        '<div class="form-group"><label>담당 지점</label><select id="bmBranchSelect"><option>서울 강남점</option><option>서울 홍대점</option><option>부산 해운대점</option><option>호치민 1호점</option><option>하노이 1호점</option></select></div>'+
        '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:24px;"><button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="promoteToManager()">지점장 추가</button><button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal()">취소</button></div>';
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
      const sel = document.getElementById('bmCandidateSelect');
      if (sel && cands.length>0) {
        sel.addEventListener('change', function(){ const emp=cands.find(e=>e.email===this.value); if(emp) document.getElementById('bmBranchSelect').value=emp.branch; });
        if(cands[0]) document.getElementById('bmBranchSelect').value=cands[0].branch;
      }
    }

    function promoteToManager() {
      const email=document.getElementById('bmCandidateSelect')?.value;
      const branch=document.getElementById('bmBranchSelect')?.value;
      if(!email||!branch){alert('직원과 지점을 선택하세요');return;}
      const emps=EmployeeStore.getAll();
      const emp=emps.find(e=>e.email===email);
      if(!emp){alert('직원을 찾을 수 없습니다');return;}
      const list=getAdminList();
      list.push({id:emp.id,name:emp.name,email:emp.email,role:'branch_manager',branch:branch});
      saveAdminList(list);
      emp.role='branch_manager';
      EmployeeStore.save(emps);
      closeModal(); renderAdminManage();
      alert(emp.name+'님이 '+branch+' 지점장으로 승격되었습니다.');
    }

    function demoteAdmin(email) {
      if(!confirm('이 지점장의 관리자 권한을 해제하시겠습니까?')) return;
      saveAdminList(getAdminList().filter(a=>a.email!==email));
      const emps=EmployeeStore.getAll();
      const emp=emps.find(e=>e.email===email);
      if(emp){emp.role='staff';EmployeeStore.save(emps);}
      renderAdminManage();
    }

    renderRoleBadge();
    applySidebarPermissions();

    // ===== 이미지 생성 중 이탈 방지 =====
    let _isGeneratingImages = false;
    window.addEventListener('beforeunload', function(e) {
      if (_isGeneratingImages) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.returnValue = '이미지 생성이 진행 중입니다. 페이지를 떠나면 생성이 중단됩니다.';
        return e.returnValue;
      }
    });

    // Supabase 초기화 + 데이터 동기화
    SupabaseMode.init().then(connected => {
      if (connected) {
        SupabaseMode.syncAll().then(() => {
          renderSopList();
          if (typeof renderTrainingReport === 'function') renderTrainingReport();
        });
      }
    });

    // ===== SOP 데이터 (localStorage + Supabase 동기화) =====
    function getSops() { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_documents') || '[]'); }
    function saveSops(sops) {
      localStorage.setItem('sop_documents', JSON.stringify(sops));
      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        SupabaseMode.saveAllSops(sops).catch(e => console.error('Admin SOP sync:', e));
      }
    }

    // 초기 데모 SOP: 사용자가 삭제한 적 없을 때만 자동 생성
    if (getSops().length === 0 && localStorage.getItem('sop_user_cleared') !== 'true') {
      if (typeof SopStore !== 'undefined') { SopStore.initDemo(); }
    }

    // ===== 현재 편집 중인 SOP =====
    let currentSopId = null;

    // ===== 페이지 전환 =====
    function showPage(page, event) {
      if (event) event.preventDefault();
      ['sop', 'content', 'dashboard', 'employees', 'learning-path', 'chat-logs', 'notifications', 'reports', 'admin-manage', 'settings', 'audit-log'].forEach(p => {
        const el = document.getElementById('page-' + p);
        if (el) el.style.display = p === page ? 'block' : 'none';
      });
      document.querySelectorAll('.admin-sidebar nav a').forEach(a => a.classList.remove('active'));
      if (event) event.currentTarget.classList.add('active');

      if (page === 'sop') renderSopList();
      if (page === 'content') renderGeneratedContent();
      if (page === 'dashboard') renderDashboard();
      if (page === 'employees') renderEmployeeManage();
      if (page === 'learning-path') renderLearningPaths();
      if (page === 'chat-logs') renderChatLogs();
      if (page === 'notifications') renderNotifHistory();
      if (page === 'reports') renderReports();
      if (page === 'admin-manage') renderAdminManage();
      if (page === 'settings') renderSettings();
      if (page === 'audit-log') renderAuditLog();

      // 모바일 사이드바 닫기
      document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
      document.getElementById('sidebarOverlay').classList.remove('show');
    }

    function toggleSidebar() {
      document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.toggle('open');
      document.getElementById('sidebarOverlay').classList.toggle('show');
    }

    // ===== SOP 필터/선택 상태 =====
    let currentSopFilter = 'all';
    let selectedSopIds = new Set();

    function updateBulkBar() {
      const bar = document.getElementById('sopBulkBar');
      if (selectedSopIds.size > 0) {
        bar.style.display = 'flex';
        document.getElementById('sopBulkCount').textContent = `${selectedSopIds.size}개 선택됨`;
      } else {
        bar.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }

    function toggleSopSelect(sopId, event) {
      event.stopPropagation();
      if (selectedSopIds.has(sopId)) selectedSopIds.delete(sopId);
      else selectedSopIds.add(sopId);
      updateBulkBar();
      // 체크박스 시각 업데이트
      const cb = document.querySelector(`.sop-checkbox[data-id="${sopId}"]`);
      if (cb) cb.checked = selectedSopIds.has(sopId);
      // 마스터 체크박스 동기화
      const total = document.querySelectorAll('.sop-checkbox').length;
      const checked = document.querySelectorAll('.sop-checkbox:checked').length;
      const masterCb = document.getElementById('sopSelectAllCheckbox');
      if (masterCb) { masterCb.checked = (checked === total && total > 0); masterCb.indeterminate = (checked > 0 && checked < total); }
    }

    function sopSelectAll() {
      let sops = getSops();
      if (currentSopFilter !== 'all') sops = sops.filter(s => s.status === currentSopFilter);
      sops.forEach(s => selectedSopIds.add(s.id));
      document.querySelectorAll('.sop-checkbox').forEach(cb => cb.checked = true);
      const masterCb = document.getElementById('sopSelectAllCheckbox');
      if (masterCb) masterCb.checked = true;
      updateBulkBar();
    }

    function sopDeselectAll() {
      selectedSopIds.clear();
      document.querySelectorAll('.sop-checkbox').forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
      const masterCb = document.getElementById('sopSelectAllCheckbox');
      if (masterCb) masterCb.checked = false;
      updateBulkBar();
    }

    function sopToggleSelectAll(checked) {
      if (checked) sopSelectAll();
      else sopDeselectAll();
    }

    function sopDeleteSelected() {
      if (selectedSopIds.size === 0) return;
      const count = selectedSopIds.size;
      if (!confirm(`선택된 ${count}개 SOP를 삭제하시겠습니까?\n\n관련 학습 진행률도 초기화됩니다.\n이 작업은 되돌릴 수 없습니다.`)) return;

      let sops = getSops();
      const deletedIds = [...selectedSopIds];
      const deletedTitles = sops.filter(s => selectedSopIds.has(s.id)).map(s => s.title).join(', ');
      sops = sops.filter(s => !selectedSopIds.has(s.id));
      saveSops(sops);
      AuditLog.add('sop', 'bulk_delete', `SOP ${count}개 일괄 삭제: ${deletedTitles}`);
      // 데모 자동 재생성 방지
      localStorage.setItem('sop_user_cleared', 'true');

      // Supabase에서도 삭제
      if (typeof SupabaseMode !== 'undefined' && SupabaseMode._ready) {
        deletedIds.forEach(id => SupabaseMode.deleteSop(id).catch(() => {}));
      }

      // 진행률 데이터 정리
      cleanupProgressData(deletedIds);

      selectedSopIds.clear();
      updateBulkBar();
      renderSopList();
      alert(`${count}개 SOP가 삭제되었습니다.`);
    }

    function sopDeleteAll() {
      const sops = getSops();
      if (sops.length === 0) { alert('삭제할 SOP가 없습니다.'); return; }
      if (!confirm(`전체 ${sops.length}개 SOP를 모두 삭제하시겠습니까?\n\n모든 학습 진행률도 초기화됩니다.\n이 작업은 되돌릴 수 없습니다.`)) return;
      if (!confirm(`정말로 전체 삭제를 진행합니까? 이 작업은 복구할 수 없습니다.`)) return;

      const deletedIds = sops.map(s => s.id);
      AuditLog.add('sop', 'delete_all', `전체 SOP ${sops.length}개 삭제`);
      saveSops([]);
      // 데모 자동 재생성 방지
      localStorage.setItem('sop_user_cleared', 'true');

      // Supabase에서도 삭제
      if (typeof SupabaseMode !== 'undefined' && SupabaseMode._ready) {
        deletedIds.forEach(id => SupabaseMode.deleteSop(id).catch(() => {}));
      }

      // 진행률 전체 초기화
      cleanupProgressData(deletedIds);

      selectedSopIds.clear();
      updateBulkBar();
      renderSopList();
      alert(`전체 ${deletedIds.length}개 SOP가 삭제되었습니다.\n새로운 SOP를 업로드하세요.`);
    }

    function cleanupProgressData(deletedSopIds) {
      // 삭제된 SOP 관련 진행률 정리
      try {
        const progressData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_progress_v2') || '{}');
        for (const empId of Object.keys(progressData)) {
          const emp = progressData[empId];
          // 삭제된 SOP의 비디오 완료 기록 제거
          emp.completedVideos = (emp.completedVideos || []).filter(vid => {
            return !deletedSopIds.some(sopId => vid.startsWith(sopId + '-'));
          });
          // 삭제된 SOP의 챕터 결과 제거
          for (const sopId of deletedSopIds) {
            delete emp.chapterResults[sopId];
            // quizScores에서도 제거
            Object.keys(emp.quizScores || {}).forEach(key => {
              if (key.startsWith(sopId + '-')) delete emp.quizScores[key];
            });
          }
        }
        localStorage.setItem('sop_progress_v2', JSON.stringify(progressData));
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('진행률 정리 오류:', e);
      }
    }

    function sopExportSelected() {
      if (selectedSopIds.size === 0) return;
      const sops = getSops().filter(s => selectedSopIds.has(s.id));
      downloadSopJson(sops, `sop-export-${selectedSopIds.size}items.json`);
    }

    function sopExportAll() {
      const sops = getSops();
      if (sops.length === 0) { alert('내보낼 SOP가 없습니다.'); return; }
      downloadSopJson(sops, `sop-export-all-${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.json`);
    }

    function downloadSopJson(sops, filename) {
      const exportData = {
        exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        version: '1.0',
        count: sops.length,
        sops: sops
      };
      const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url; a.download = filename;
      document.body.appendChild(a); a.click();
      document.body.removeChild(a);
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    }

    // ===== 선택 SOP 이미지 일괄 생성 =====
    async function sopBulkGenerateImages() {
      if (selectedSopIds.size === 0) { alert('SOP를 먼저 선택하세요.'); return; }
      _isGeneratingImages = true;
      const sops = getSops();
      const targets = sops.filter(s => selectedSopIds.has(s.id) && s.script && s.script.length > 0);

      if (targets.length === 0) {
        alert('선택된 SOP 중 스크립트가 있는 SOP가 없습니다.\n먼저 각 SOP의 스크립트를 생성해주세요.');
        return;
      }

      const totalScenes = targets.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.script.filter(sc => !sc.imageConfirmed).length, 0);
      if (totalScenes === 0) {
        alert('모든 씬의 이미지가 이미 확정되었습니다.');
        return;
      }

      if (!confirm(`${targets.length}개 SOP의 이미지를 일괄 생성합니다.\n\n총 ${totalScenes}개 씬\n예상 비용: ~$${(totalScenes * 0.04).toFixed(2)}\n\n진행하시겠습니까?`)) return;

      // 프로그레스 모달
      const overlay = document.createElement('div');
      overlay.id = 'bulkImageModal';
      overlay.className = 'modal-overlay show';
      overlay.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal" style="max-width:500px; text-align:center;">
          <h3>🎨 전체 SOP 이미지 생성</h3>
          <div id="bulkSopProgress" style="margin:20px 0;"></div>
          <div style="background:#e2e8f0; border-radius:8px; height:10px; overflow:hidden; margin:16px 0;">
            <div id="bulkBar" style="background:linear-gradient(90deg,#6366f1,#8b5cf6); height:100%; width:0%; transition:width 0.3s;"></div>
          </div>
          <div id="bulkCount" style="font-size:14px; color:var(--gray-600);">0 / ${totalScenes} 이미지</div>
          <div id="bulkSopName" style="font-size:13px; color:var(--gray-400); margin-top:8px;"></div>
        </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(overlay);

      let done = 0;
      const BATCH_SIZE = 3;

      for (const sop of targets) {
        const sopIdx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === sop.id);
        document.getElementById('bulkSopName').textContent = `📋 ${sop.title}`;

        const sceneJobs = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < sop.script.length; i++) {
          if (!sop.script[i].imageConfirmed) sceneJobs.push(i);
        }

        for (let b = 0; b < sceneJobs.length; b += BATCH_SIZE) {
          const batch = sceneJobs.slice(b, b + BATCH_SIZE);

          await Promise.all(batch.map(async (i) => {
            const scene = sop.script[i];
            try {
              const imgRes = await fetch('/api/image', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'generate-multi', visual: scene.visual || '', narration: scene.narration, sceneIndex: i, totalScenes: sop.script.length })
              });
              const imgData = await imgRes.json();
              if (imgData.images && imgData.images.length > 0 && imgData.images[0].imageUrl) {
                scene.imageUrl = imgData.images[0].imageUrl;
              }
            } catch (e) { console.warn(`이미지 실패: ${sop.title} 씬${i+1}`, e.message); }

            done++;
            document.getElementById('bulkCount').textContent = `${done} / ${totalScenes} 이미지`;
            document.getElementById('bulkBar').style.width = (done / totalScenes * 100) + '%';
          }));

          saveSops(sops);
          if (b + BATCH_SIZE < sceneJobs.length) await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000));
        }
      }

      saveSops(sops);
      _isGeneratingImages = false;
      document.getElementById('bulkImageModal').remove();
      alert(`✅ 완료! ${done}개 이미지 생성됨`);
      renderSopList();
    }

    // ===== JSON 일괄 업로드 =====
    async function handleSopJsonUpload(event) {
      const file = event.target.files?.[0];
      if (!file) return;
      event.target.value = '';

      try {
        const text = await file.text();
        const data = JSON.parse(text);

        // 다양한 JSON 형식 지원
        let newSops = [];
        if (Array.isArray(data)) {
          newSops = data;
        } else if (data.sops && Array.isArray(data.sops)) {
          newSops = data.sops;
        } else if (data.title && data.content) {
          newSops = [data]; // 단일 SOP 객체
        } else {
          alert('지원하지 않는 JSON 형식입니다.\n배열 또는 { sops: [...] } 형식이어야 합니다.');
          return;
        }

        if (newSops.length === 0) {
          alert('업로드할 SOP가 없습니다.'); return;
        }

        // 기존 SOP 처리 선택
        const existingSops = getSops();
        let mode = 'append';
        if (existingSops.length > 0) {
          const choice = confirm(
            `현재 ${existingSops.length}개 SOP가 있습니다.\n\n` +
            `[확인] = 기존 SOP를 모두 삭제하고 새로 교체 (${newSops.length}개)\n` +
            `[취소] = 기존 SOP에 추가 (${existingSops.length} + ${newSops.length}개)`
          );
          mode = choice ? 'replace' : 'append';
        }

        // SOP 정규화 (필수 필드 보장)
        const normalized = newSops.map((sop, i) => ({
          id: sop.id || ('sop-' + Date.now() + '-' + i),
          title: sop.title || `SOP ${i + 1}`,
          title_en: sop.title_en || null,
          title_vn: sop.title_vn || null,
          category: sop.category || '기타',
          content: sop.content || '',
          content_vn: sop.content_vn || '',
          status: sop.status || 'draft',
          order_num: sop.order_num || (i + 1),
          createdAt: sop.createdAt || new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),
          script: sop.script || null,
          quizzes: sop.quizzes || null,
        }));

        if (mode === 'replace') {
          // 기존 진행률도 정리
          const deletedIds = existingSops.map(s => s.id);
          cleanupProgressData(deletedIds);
          if (typeof SupabaseMode !== 'undefined' && SupabaseMode._ready) {
            deletedIds.forEach(id => SupabaseMode.deleteSop(id).catch(() => {}));
          }
          saveSops(normalized);
        } else {
          saveSops([...existingSops, ...normalized]);
        }
        // 새 SOP가 업로드되었으므로 자동 생성 차단 유지 (데모 재생성 방지)
        localStorage.setItem('sop_user_cleared', 'true');

        selectedSopIds.clear();
        updateBulkBar();
        renderSopList();

        const modeLabel = mode === 'replace' ? '교체' : '추가';
        alert(`${normalized.length}개 SOP가 ${modeLabel}되었습니다.`);

      } catch (e) {
        console.error('JSON 업로드 오류:', e);
        alert(`JSON 파일 처리 오류:\n${e.message}`);
      }
    }

    // ===== SOP 목록 렌더링 =====
    function renderSopList() {
      document.getElementById('sopListView').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('sopEditorView').style.display = 'none';

      let sops = getSops();
      if (currentSopFilter !== 'all') {
        sops = sops.filter(s => s.status === currentSopFilter);
      }
      const container = document.getElementById('sopList');

      const listHeader = document.getElementById('sopListHeader');
      if (sops.length === 0) {
        listHeader.style.display = 'none';
        container.innerHTML = `
          <div style="text-align:center; padding:60px; color:var(--gray-500);">
            <p style="font-size:48px; margin-bottom:12px;">&#128221;</p>
            <p style="font-size:16px; font-weight:600; margin-bottom:4px;">아직 작성된 SOP가 없습니다</p>
            <p style="font-size:14px;">위의 "새 SOP 작성" 또는 "JSON 일괄 업로드" 버튼으로 시작하세요</p>
          </div>`;
        updateBulkBar();
        return;
      }
      listHeader.style.display = 'flex';
      document.getElementById('sopCountLabel').textContent = `총 ${sops.length}개`;
      // 마스터 체크박스 동기화
      const allChecked = sops.every(s => selectedSopIds.has(s.id));
      document.getElementById('sopSelectAllCheckbox').checked = allChecked;

      container.innerHTML = sops.map(sop => {
        const statusMap = {
          draft: { label: '작성 중', color: 'var(--gray-500)', bg: 'var(--gray-100)' },
          generated: { label: 'AI 생성 완료', color: 'var(--primary)', bg: 'var(--primary-light)' },
          reviewed: { label: '검토 완료', color: '#92400e', bg: '#fef3c7' },
          published: { label: '배포됨', color: 'var(--success)', bg: '#dcfce7' },
        };
        const st = statusMap[sop.status] || statusMap.draft;
        const hasScript = sop.script && sop.script.length > 0;
        const hasQuiz = sop.quizzes && sop.quizzes.length > 0;
        const isChecked = selectedSopIds.has(sop.id);

        return `
          <div class="sop-list-item" style="position:relative;">
            <input type="checkbox" class="sop-checkbox" data-id="${sop.id}"
              ${isChecked ? 'checked' : ''}
              onclick="toggleSopSelect('${sop.id}', event)"
              style="width:18px; height:18px; cursor:pointer; flex-shrink:0; accent-color:var(--primary);">
            <div class="sop-icon" style="background:${st.bg}; color:${st.color};" onclick="openSopEditor('${sop.id}')">&#128221;</div>
            <div class="sop-info" onclick="openSopEditor('${sop.id}')" style="cursor:pointer;">
              <h4>${sop.title}</h4>
              <p>${sop.category || ''} · ${sop.createdAt || ''}</p>
              <div class="sop-badges" style="margin-top:6px;">
                <span class="badge" style="background:${st.bg}; color:${st.color};">${st.label}</span>
                ${hasScript ? '<span class="badge" style="background:var(--primary-light); color:var(--primary);">스크립트 ✓</span>' : ''}
                ${hasQuiz ? '<span class="badge" style="background:#dcfce7; color:var(--success);">퀴즈 ' + sop.quizzes.length + '문제</span>' : ''}
              </div>
            </div>
            <span style="color:var(--gray-300); cursor:pointer;" onclick="openSopEditor('${sop.id}')">&#8250;</span>
          </div>`;
      }).join('');
      updateBulkBar();
    }

    function filterSop(status, btn) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.filter-chip').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
      btn.classList.add('active');
      currentSopFilter = status;
      selectedSopIds.clear();
      renderSopList();
    }

    // ===== 파일 업로드 → SOP 변환 =====
    async function handleSopFileUpload(event) {
      if (!hasPermission('sop_create')) { alert('SOP 생성 권한이 없습니다.'); return; }
      const files = event.target.files;
      if (!files || files.length === 0) return;

      let successCount = 0;
      for (const file of files) {
        showLoading(`파일 읽는 중: ${file.name}`);

        try {
          let text = '';

          if (file.name.endsWith('.txt') || file.name.endsWith('.md')) {
            text = await file.text();
          } else if (file.name.endsWith('.pdf')) {
            text = await extractPdfText(file);
          } else if (file.name.endsWith('.doc') || file.name.endsWith('.docx')) {
            text = await extractDocText(file);
          } else if (file.name.endsWith('.hwp')) {
            text = await file.text(); // HWP는 텍스트만 추출 시도
          } else {
            text = await file.text();
          }

          if (!text || text.trim().length < 20) {
            alert(`"${file.name}" 에서 텍스트를 추출할 수 없습니다.\nTXT 파일로 변환 후 다시 시도해주세요.`);
            continue;
          }

          // 원문 그대로 저장 (AI 구조화 없음)
          const sops = getSops();
          const title = file.name.replace(/\.[^/.]+$/, '');
          // 줄 단위로 bullet 리스트 생성 (번호 없이)
          const lines = text.split(/\r?\n/).filter(l => l.trim().length > 0);
          const rawHtml = '<ul>' + lines.map(l => `<li>${l.trim()}</li>`).join('') + '</ul>';
          const newSop = {
            id: 'sop-' + Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2,4),
            title: title,
            category: '기타',
            chapter: 'new',
            status: 'draft',
            content: rawHtml,
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),
            script: null,
            quizzes: null
          };
          sops.push(newSop);
          saveSops(sops);
          successCount++;

        } catch (e) {
          console.error('File upload error:', e);
          alert(`"${file.name}" 처리 중 오류: ${e.message}`);
        }
      }

      hideLoading();
      renderSopList();
      event.target.value = ''; // 파일 입력 초기화
      if (successCount > 0) {
        alert(`${successCount}개 파일이 SOP로 변환되었습니다.\n클릭하여 내용을 확인하고 AI 콘텐츠를 생성하세요.`);
      } else {
        alert(`파일 변환에 실패했습니다.\nTXT 파일로 변환 후 다시 시도하거나, 직접 작성해주세요.`);
      }
    }

    // ===== 폴더 업로드 =====
    async function handleSopFolderUpload(event) {
      const files = Array.from(event.target.files).filter(f =>
        /\.(txt|md|pdf|doc|docx|hwp)$/i.test(f.name) && !f.name.startsWith('.')
      );
      if (!files.length) { alert('지원되는 파일이 없습니다 (TXT, PDF, Word, HWP)'); return; }
      await processMultipleFiles(files);
      event.target.value = '';
    }

    // ===== 드래그앤드롭 =====
    async function handleSopDrop(event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      const items = event.dataTransfer.items;
      const files = [];
      const jsonFiles = [];

      async function traverseEntry(entry) {
        if (entry.isFile) {
          const file = await new Promise(resolve => entry.file(resolve));
          if (/\.json$/i.test(file.name)) jsonFiles.push(file);
          else if (/\.(txt|md|pdf|doc|docx|hwp)$/i.test(file.name)) files.push(file);
        } else if (entry.isDirectory) {
          const reader = entry.createReader();
          const entries = await new Promise(resolve => reader.readEntries(resolve));
          for (const e of entries) await traverseEntry(e);
        }
      }

      showLoading('파일 탐색 중...');
      for (const item of items) {
        const entry = item.webkitGetAsEntry ? item.webkitGetAsEntry() : null;
        if (entry) await traverseEntry(entry);
        else if (item.kind === 'file') {
          const file = item.getAsFile();
          if (/\.json$/i.test(file.name)) jsonFiles.push(file);
          else if (/\.(txt|md|pdf|doc|docx|hwp)$/i.test(file.name)) files.push(file);
        }
      }
      hideLoading();

      // JSON 파일 우선 처리
      if (jsonFiles.length > 0) {
        const fakeEvent = { target: { files: jsonFiles, value: '' } };
        await handleSopJsonUpload(fakeEvent);
        return;
      }

      if (!files.length) { alert('지원되는 파일이 없습니다 (TXT, PDF, Word, HWP, JSON)'); return; }
      await processMultipleFiles(files);
    }

    // ===== 다중 파일 → AI 자동 챕터 분류 =====
    async function processMultipleFiles(files) {
      showLoading(`${files.length}개 파일 읽는 중...`);

      // 1. 모든 파일 텍스트 추출
      const fileContents = [];
      for (const file of files) {
        try {
          showLoading(`텍스트 추출 중: ${file.name}`);
          let text = '';
          if (/\.(txt|md|hwp)$/i.test(file.name)) text = await file.text();
          else if (/\.pdf$/i.test(file.name)) text = await extractPdfText(file);
          else if (/\.(doc|docx)$/i.test(file.name)) text = await extractDocText(file);
          if (text && text.trim().length > 10) {
            // 폴더 경로에서 카테고리 추출
            const pathParts = (file.webkitRelativePath || file.name).split('/');
            const folder = pathParts.length > 1 ? pathParts[pathParts.length - 2] : '';
            fileContents.push({ name: file.name, folder, text: text.slice(0, 2000) });
          }
        } catch(e) { console.error('Extract error:', file.name, e); }
      }

      if (!fileContents.length) { hideLoading(); alert('텍스트를 추출할 수 있는 파일이 없습니다.'); return; }

      // 2. AI로 챕터 자동 분류
      showLoading(`AI가 ${fileContents.length}개 파일을 챕터별로 분류 중...`);
      let organized;
      try {
        organized = await aiOrganizeFiles(fileContents);
      } catch(e) {
        console.error('AI organize error:', e);
        // 폴백: 폴더명 또는 파일명 기준 분류
        organized = fallbackOrganize(fileContents);
      }

      // 3. SOP로 저장
      const sops = getSops();
      const chapters = (typeof SopStore !== 'undefined' && SopStore.getChapters) ? SopStore.getChapters() : JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_chapters_custom') || '[]');
      let created = 0;

      for (const group of organized) {
        // 챕터가 없으면 생성
        let chapterId = chapters.find(c => c.title === group.chapter)?.id;
        if (!chapterId) {
          chapterId = 'ch-' + Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2,4);
          const newChapter = { id: chapterId, title: group.chapter, order: chapters.length + 1 };
          chapters.push(newChapter);
          localStorage.setItem('sop_chapters_custom', JSON.stringify(chapters));
        }

        const newSop = {
          id: 'sop-' + Date.now() + '-' + (++created) + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2,3),
          title: group.title,
          category: group.category || '기타',
          chapter: chapterId,
          status: 'draft',
          content: group.html,
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),
          script: null, quizzes: null
        };
        sops.push(newSop);
      }

      saveSops(sops);
      hideLoading();
      renderSopList();
      alert(`${created}개 SOP가 생성되었습니다.\n\nAI가 다음과 같이 분류했습니다:\n${organized.map(g => `• [${g.chapter}] ${g.title}`).join('\n')}\n\n각 SOP를 확인하고 "AI 콘텐츠 생성"을 클릭하세요.`);
    }

    // AI 파일 분류
    async function aiOrganizeFiles(fileContents) {
      const fileList = fileContents.map((f, i) => `[${i}] "${f.name}" (폴더: ${f.folder || '없음'})\n내용 미리보기: ${f.text.slice(0, 300)}`).join('\n\n');

      const prompt = `다음 ${fileContents.length}개의 교육 자료 파일을 SOP 챕터별로 분류하고 구조화해주세요.

파일 목록:
${fileList}

규칙:
1. 관련된 파일끼리 하나의 챕터로 묶으세요
2. 각 챕터에는 명확한 제목을 붙이세요 (예: "출근 및 매장 오픈", "고객 응대", "안전 관리")
3. 각 파일의 내용을 SOP HTML로 구조화하세요
4. 카테고리: 오프닝/고객 응대/안전·위생/클로징/비상 대응/기타

JSON 배열로 응답:
[{"chapter":"챕터명","title":"SOP 제목","category":"카테고리","html":"<h3>1. 절차</h3><ol><li>내용</li></ol>","fileIndices":[0,1]}]`;

      const aiText = await callGemini(prompt, { temperature: 0.5, maxOutputTokens: 4096 });
      const jsonMatch = aiText.match(/\[[\s\S]*\]/);
      if (jsonMatch) return JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
      throw new Error('AI 응답 파싱 실패');
    }

    // 폴백: 폴더명/파일명 기준 분류
    function fallbackOrganize(fileContents) {
      const groups = {};
      fileContents.forEach(f => {
        const key = f.folder || '일반';
        if (!groups[key]) groups[key] = [];
        groups[key].push(f);
      });

      return Object.entries(groups).map(([folder, items]) => ({
        chapter: folder === '일반' ? '교육 자료' : folder,
        title: items.length === 1 ? items[0].name.replace(/\.[^/.]+$/, '') : `${folder} SOP`,
        category: '기타',
        html: items.map(f => `<h3>${f.name.replace(/\.[^/.]+$/, '')}</h3><p>${f.text.replace(/\n\n/g, '</p><p>').replace(/\n/g, '<br>')}</p>`).join('\n')
      }));
    }

    // PDF 텍스트 추출 (pdf.js CDN)
    async function extractPdfText(file) {
      try {
        if (!window.pdfjsLib) {
          showLoading('PDF 라이브러리 로딩 중...');
          const script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.min.js';
          document.head.appendChild(script);
          await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            script.onload = resolve;
            script.onerror = () => reject(new Error('PDF 라이브러리 로드 실패'));
          });
          pdfjsLib.GlobalWorkerOptions.workerSrc = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/pdf.js/3.11.174/pdf.worker.min.js';
        }

        const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
        const pdf = await pdfjsLib.getDocument({ data: arrayBuffer }).promise;
        let text = '';
        for (let i = 1; i <= pdf.numPages; i++) {
          const page = await pdf.getPage(i);
          const content = await page.getTextContent();
          text += content.items.map(item => item.str).join(' ') + '\n\n';
        }
        return text;
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('PDF extraction error:', e);
        return '';
      }
    }

    // Word(docx) 텍스트 추출 (mammoth.js CDN)
    async function extractDocText(file) {
      try {
        if (!window.mammoth) {
          showLoading('Word 라이브러리 로딩 중...');
          const script = document.createElement('script');
          script.src = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/mammoth/1.6.0/mammoth.browser.min.js';
          document.head.appendChild(script);
          await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            script.onload = resolve;
            script.onerror = () => reject(new Error('Word 라이브러리 로드 실패'));
          });
        }

        const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
        const result = await mammoth.convertToHtml({ arrayBuffer });
        return result.value; // 이미 HTML 형태
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('DOCX extraction error:', e);
        return '';
      }
    }

    // AI로 텍스트 → SOP 구조화
    async function convertTextToSop(text, filename) {
      // Gemini가 설정되어 있으면 AI 변환
      if (AI_CONFIG.scriptProvider === 'gemini' || AI_CONFIG.quizProvider === 'gemini') {
        try {
          const prompt = `다음 텍스트를 SOP(표준운영절차) 형식의 HTML로 구조화해주세요.

규칙:
1. 제목을 추출하세요
2. 절차를 단계별로 <h3>번호. 단계명</h3><ol><li>상세 내용</li></ol> 형식으로 정리
3. 주의사항은 <p><strong>⚠️ 주의:</strong> 내용</p>으로 표시
4. 카테고리를 추정하세요 (오프닝/고객 응대/안전·위생/클로징/비상 대응/기타 중 하나)

JSON으로 응답: {"title":"제목","category":"카테고리","html":"<h3>1. ...</h3><ol>..."}

텍스트:
${text.slice(0, 3000)}`;

          const aiText = await callGemini(prompt);

          // JSON 추출
          const jsonMatch = aiText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
          if (jsonMatch) {
            return JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('AI SOP conversion error:', e);
        }
      }

      // 폴백: 단순 텍스트 → HTML 변환
      const lines = text.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
      let html = '';
      let stepNum = 1;
      lines.forEach(line => {
        line = line.trim();
        if (line.length > 30 && stepNum === 1) {
          // 첫 긴 줄은 건너뛰기 (제목일 수 있음)
        }
        if (/^\d+[\.\)]\s/.test(line) || /^[가-힣]+\s*\d/.test(line)) {
          html += `<h3>${stepNum}. ${line.replace(/^\d+[\.\)]\s*/, '')}</h3><ol>`;
          stepNum++;
        } else if (line.length > 5) {
          html += `<li>${line}</li>`;
        }
      });

      return {
        title: filename.replace(/\.[^/.]+$/, ''),
        category: '기타',
        html: html || `<p>${text.replace(/\n\n/g, '</p><p>').replace(/\n/g, '<br>')}</p>`
      };
    }

    // ===== 새 SOP 생성 =====
    function createNewSop() {
      if (!hasPermission('sop_create')) { alert('SOP 생성 권한이 없습니다.'); return; }
      const sops = getSops();
      const newSop = {
        id: 'sop-' + Date.now(),
        title: '새 SOP',
        category: '기타',
        chapter: 'new',
        status: 'draft',
        content: '<h3>1. 첫 번째 절차</h3><ol><li>여기에 상세 단계를 입력하세요</li><li>구체적일수록 AI가 더 좋은 스크립트를 생성합니다</li></ol><h3>2. 두 번째 절차</h3><ol><li>단계를 추가하세요</li></ol>',
        createdAt: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10),
        script: null,
        quizzes: null
      };
      sops.push(newSop);
      saveSops(sops);
      AuditLog.add('sop', 'create', `새 SOP 생성: "${newSop.title}"`);
      openSopEditor(newSop.id);
    }

    // ===== SOP 에디터 열기 =====
    function openSopEditor(sopId) {
      currentSopId = sopId;
      const sops = getSops();
      const sop = sops.find(s => s.id === sopId);
      if (!sop) return;

      document.getElementById('sopListView').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('sopEditorView').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('sopTitleInput').value = sop.title;
      document.getElementById('sopEditor').innerHTML = sop.content;
      document.getElementById('sopCategory').value = sop.category || '기타';

      // 상태 플로우
      renderStatusFlow(sop.status);

      // AI 결과 표시
      renderAiResults(sop);

      // 지점장: 편집 불가 (읽기 전용)
      if (!hasPermission('sop_edit')) {
        document.getElementById('sopEditor').setAttribute('contenteditable', 'false');
        document.getElementById('sopTitleInput').readOnly = true;
        document.querySelector('.editor-toolbar').style.display = 'none';
        document.querySelector('#sopEditorView .topbar-actions').style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        document.getElementById('sopEditor').setAttribute('contenteditable', 'true');
        document.getElementById('sopTitleInput').readOnly = false;
        document.querySelector('.editor-toolbar').style.display = 'flex';
        document.querySelector('#sopEditorView .topbar-actions').style.display = 'flex';
      }

      window.scrollTo(0, 0);
    }

    function deleteSop() {
      if (!hasPermission('sop_delete')) { alert('SOP 삭제 권한이 없습니다.'); return; }
      if (!currentSopId) return;
      if (!confirm('이 SOP를 삭제하시겠습니까? 이 작업은 되돌릴 수 없습니다.')) return;
      const deletedId = currentSopId;
      const deletedSop = getSops().find(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      const sops = getSops().filter(s => s.id !== currentSopId);
      AuditLog.add('sop', 'delete', `SOP 삭제: "${deletedSop?.title || deletedId}"`);
      saveSops(sops);
      // 데모 자동 재생성 방지 + 진행률 정리
      localStorage.setItem('sop_user_cleared', 'true');
      cleanupProgressData([deletedId]);
      if (typeof SupabaseMode !== 'undefined' && SupabaseMode._ready) {
        SupabaseMode.deleteSop(deletedId).catch(() => {});
      }
      currentSopId = null;
      document.getElementById('sopListView').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('sopEditorView').style.display = 'none';
      renderSopList();
    }

    function closeSopEditor() {
      saveSop();
      document.getElementById('sopListView').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('sopEditorView').style.display = 'none';
      currentSopId = null;
      renderSopList();
    }

    function renderStatusFlow(status) {
      const steps = [
        { key: 'draft', label: 'SOP 작성' },
        { key: 'generated', label: 'AI 생성' },
        { key: 'reviewed', label: '검토' },
        { key: 'published', label: '배포' },
      ];
      const statusOrder = ['draft', 'generated', 'reviewed', 'published'];
      const currentIdx = statusOrder.indexOf(status);

      document.getElementById('sopStatusFlow').innerHTML = steps.map((s, i) => {
        let cls = 'pending';
        if (i < currentIdx) cls = 'done';
        if (i === currentIdx) cls = 'current';
        return `${i > 0 ? '<span class="flow-arrow">→</span>' : ''}
          <span class="flow-step ${cls}">${cls === 'done' ? '✓ ' : ''}${s.label}</span>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    // ===== SOP 저장 =====
    function saveSop() {
      if (!currentSopId) return;
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      const newTitle = document.getElementById('sopTitleInput').value || '제목 없음';
      const newContent = document.getElementById('sopEditor').innerHTML;
      const newCategory = document.getElementById('sopCategory').value;

      // Save version snapshot if content or title changed
      if (sops[idx].title !== newTitle || sops[idx].content !== newContent) {
        saveVersionSnapshot(currentSopId, {
          title: newTitle,
          content: newContent,
          category: newCategory
        });
        AuditLog.add('sop', 'edit', `SOP 수정: "${newTitle}"`);
      }

      sops[idx].title = newTitle;
      sops[idx].content = newContent;
      sops[idx].category = newCategory;
      // 챕터 선택도 저장
      const chapterSelect = document.getElementById('sopChapterSelect');
      if (chapterSelect) sops[idx].chapter = chapterSelect.value;
      saveSops(sops);
    }

    // ===== 에디터 명령 =====
    function execCmd(cmd) { document.execCommand(cmd, false, null); }
    function insertHeading() { document.execCommand('formatBlock', false, 'h3'); }
    function insertStep() {
      const num = document.getElementById('sopEditor').querySelectorAll('h3').length + 1;
      document.execCommand('insertHTML', false,
        `<h3>${num}. 새 절차</h3><ul><li>단계를 입력하세요</li></ul>`);
    }
    function insertWarning() {
      document.execCommand('insertHTML', false,
        '<p><strong>⚠️ 주의:</strong> 주의사항을 입력하세요</p>');
    }

    // 붙여넣기 시 원문 그대로 유지 (자동 번호/포맷 제거)
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const editor = document.getElementById('sopEditor');
      if (!editor) return;
      editor.addEventListener('paste', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        const text = e.clipboardData.getData('text/plain');
        // 줄 단위로 분리 → 각 줄을 <li>로 변환 (번호 없는 bullet)
        const lines = text.split(/\r?\n/).filter(l => l.trim().length > 0);
        const html = '<ul>' + lines.map(l => `<li>${l.trim()}</li>`).join('') + '</ul>';
        document.execCommand('insertHTML', false, html);
      });
    });

    // ===== 로딩 오버레이 =====
    function showLoading(msg) {
      let overlay = document.getElementById('loadingOverlay');
      if (!overlay) {
        overlay = document.createElement('div');
        overlay.id = 'loadingOverlay';
        overlay.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.5);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;z-index:10000;';
        overlay.innerHTML = '<div style="background:white;padding:32px 48px;border-radius:16px;text-align:center;"><div class="spinner" style="margin:0 auto 16px;width:40px;height:40px;border:4px solid #e2e8f0;border-top-color:#2563eb;border-radius:50%;animation:spin 1s linear infinite;"></div><p id="loadingText" style="font-size:15px;color:#334155;"></p></div>';
        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = '@keyframes spin{to{transform:rotate(360deg)}}';
        document.head.appendChild(style);
        document.body.appendChild(overlay);
      }
      document.getElementById('loadingText').textContent = msg || '처리 중...';
      overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    }
    function hideLoading() {
      const overlay = document.getElementById('loadingOverlay');
      if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // ===== AI 콘텐츠 생성 (SOP 원문 → 스크립트, AI → 퀴즈만) =====
    function generateContent() {
      if (!hasPermission('sop_edit')) { alert('SOP 편집 권한이 없습니다.'); return; }
      saveSop();
      const sops = getSops();
      const sop = sops.find(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (!sop) return;

      const content = sop.content;
      if (content.length < 50) {
        alert('SOP 내용이 너무 짧습니다. 좀 더 상세하게 작성해주세요.');
        return;
      }

      // 로딩 표시
      document.getElementById('aiResultArea').innerHTML = `
        <div class="ai-result-section" style="margin-top:20px;">
          <div class="generating-overlay">
            <div class="big-spinner"></div>
            <h3 style="margin-bottom:4px;">콘텐츠를 생성하고 있습니다...</h3>
            <p style="color:var(--gray-500); font-size:14px;">SOP 원문으로 슬라이드를 구성하고 퀴즈를 생성합니다</p>
          </div>
        </div>`;

      document.getElementById('generateBtn').disabled = true;

      (async () => {
        try {
          // ① SOP 원문을 그대로 씬으로 분할 (AI 호출 없음)
          showLoading('SOP 원문으로 스크립트 구성 중...');
          console.log('[generateContent] SOP content length:', sop.content.length);
          console.log('[generateContent] SOP content preview:', sop.content.substring(0, 200));
          const scriptResult = _sopContentToScenes(sop.content);
          console.log('[generateContent] 생성된 씬 수:', scriptResult.length);
          if (scriptResult.length > 0) {
            console.log('[generateContent] 씬1:', scriptResult[0].narration.substring(0, 50));
            if (scriptResult.length > 1) console.log('[generateContent] 씬2:', scriptResult[1].narration.substring(0, 50));
          }

          // ② AI는 퀴즈만 생성
          showLoading('AI 퀴즈 생성 중...');
          const quizResult = await AI.generateQuiz(sop.title, sop.content);

          hideLoading();

          const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
          sops[idx].script = scriptResult;
          sops[idx].quizzes = quizResult;
          sops[idx].status = 'generated';
          saveSops(sops);

          // 이전 캐시 초기화 (새 스크립트에 맞는 새 이미지/음성 생성)
          localStorage.removeItem('sop_image_cache_v1');
          localStorage.removeItem('sop_tts_cache_v1');

          renderStatusFlow('generated');
          renderAiResults(sops[idx]);

          const autoImage = confirm(`✅ 완료!\n\n📋 슬라이드: ${scriptResult.length}씬 (SOP 원문 기반)\n📝 퀴즈: ${quizResult.length}문제 (AI 생성)\n\n이미지도 바로 생성할까요?`);
          if (autoImage) {
            setTimeout(() => _generateAllImages(), 500);
          }
        } catch (e) {
          hideLoading();
          alert('생성 중 오류: ' + e.message);
        } finally {
          document.getElementById('generateBtn').disabled = false;
          document.getElementById('generateBtn').innerHTML = '&#128260; 다시 생성';
        }
      })();
    }

    // SOP 원문 HTML을 슬라이드 씬 배열로 변환 (bullet 1개 = 씬 1개)
    function _sopContentToScenes(htmlContent) {
      const temp = document.createElement('div');
      temp.innerHTML = htmlContent;

      // li 태그가 있으면 li 기준, 없으면 줄 기준
      const lis = temp.querySelectorAll('li');
      let lines = [];
      if (lis.length > 0) {
        lis.forEach(li => {
          const t = li.textContent.trim();
          if (t.length > 0) lines.push(t);
        });
      } else {
        const text = temp.textContent || temp.innerText || '';
        lines = text.split(/\n+/).map(l => l.trim()).filter(l => l.length > 0);
      }

      if (lines.length === 0) return [];

      // 원문 그대로 사용 — 가공하지 않음
      // 각 줄 = 1씬 (빈 줄만 제외)
      return lines.map((narration, i) => ({
        scene: i + 1,
        narration: narration,
        visual: `Scene ${i + 1}: Training content slide`,
        imageUrl: null
      }));
    }

    // ===== 스크립트 편집 함수 =====
    window._saveScripts = function() {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      const textareas = document.querySelectorAll('.scene-narration');
      const oldScript = sops[idx].script || [];
      const newScript = [];
      const emptyScenes = [];
      textareas.forEach((ta, i) => {
        const text = ta.value.trim();
        const old = oldScript[i] || {};
        if (text.length > 0) {
          newScript.push({
            scene: i + 1,
            narration: text,
            visual: old.visual || `Scene ${i + 1}: Training content slide`,
            imageUrl: old.imageUrl || null,
            imageConfirmed: old.imageConfirmed || false,
          });
        } else if (old.imageUrl) {
          emptyScenes.push(i + 1);
        }
      });

      // 이미지가 있는 빈 씬 경고
      if (emptyScenes.length > 0 && !confirm(`씬 ${emptyScenes.join(', ')}에 이미지가 있지만 텍스트가 비어있어 삭제됩니다. 계속할까요?`)) return;

      newScript.forEach((s, i) => s.scene = i + 1);

      sops[idx].script = newScript;
      saveSops(sops);

      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
      alert(`✅ ${newScript.length}개 씬 저장 완료\n\n이미지를 생성하려면 "🎨 이미지 일괄 생성" 버튼을 눌러주세요.`);
    }

    // ===== 개별 씬 이미지 생성 =====
    // ===== 이미지 프롬프트 생성 템플릿 =====
    // === 로컬 프롬프트 변환 (공유 모듈 scene-prompts.js 사용) ===
    function _localPromptFromNarration(narration) {
      // 공유 모듈이 로드되었으면 사용 (Single Source of Truth)
      if (window.ScenePrompts) {
        return window.ScenePrompts.narrationToPrompt(narration, '', { withCamera: true });
      }
      // fallback (scene-prompts.js 로드 실패 시)
      const text = narration.toLowerCase();
      const cameras = ['Wide shot.', 'Medium shot.', 'Close-up shot.', 'Over-the-shoulder shot.'];
      const cam = cameras[Math.floor(Math.random() * cameras.length)];

      // 키워드 → 구체적 영어 장면
      const scenes = [
        // 위생/손씻기
        { kw: ['손 씻', '손씻', 'hand wash', '비누', 'soap'], en: 'A young Korean woman in a light blue apron carefully washing her hands with soap and water under a stainless steel faucet. Clean modern kitchen with white tiles and bright lighting.' },
        { kw: ['손바닥', '문질러', '문지르'], en: 'Close-up of two hands rubbing palms together under running water with soap bubbles. Clean sink area with bright overhead lighting.' },
        { kw: ['손가락', '손톱', '엄지'], en: 'Close-up of hands carefully cleaning between fingers and under fingernails with soap. Bright clean washroom.' },
        { kw: ['세균', '감염', '예방', '위생', '균'], en: 'A colorful educational infographic poster about germs and hygiene displayed on a clean white wall. Bright classroom setting with warm lighting.' },
        // 인사/환영
        { kw: ['인사', '환영', '안녕', 'greeting', 'welcome'], en: 'A smiling young Korean woman in neat beige uniform bowing warmly to welcome visitors at a bright modern reception desk with plants.' },
        // 교육/가치
        { kw: ['교육', '철학', '가치', '핵심', '믿음'], en: 'A young Korean woman in smart casual clothes sitting at a round wooden table, thoughtfully reading an open book. Cozy meeting room with bookshelves and warm lighting.' },
        // 아이/어린이
        { kw: ['아이', '어린이', '유아', '아동', 'child', 'kid'], en: 'A friendly Korean woman in a colorful apron kneeling down to eye level with small happy children in a bright playroom with colorful toys.' },
        // 청소/위생
        { kw: ['청소', '소독', '닦', '쓸', 'clean'], en: 'A person in a clean uniform wiping down a table surface with a spray bottle and cloth. Bright tidy room with organized shelves.' },
        // 점검
        { kw: ['점검', '체크', '확인', 'check', 'inspect'], en: 'A young Korean woman in uniform holding a clipboard and checking items on a checklist. Well-organized storage room with labeled shelves.' },
        // 안전
        { kw: ['안전', '주의', '위험', 'safety'], en: 'A safety instruction sign on a wall next to well-organized equipment. Bright clean facility with safety markings on the floor.' },
        // 출근/시작

      for (const s of scenes) {
        if (s.kw.some(k => text.includes(k))) {

      }

      // 매칭 안 되면 일반적 교육 장면

    function _buildImagePrompt(narration) {
      // SOP 제목에서 환경 자동 감지
      const sops = getSops();
      const sidx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      const sopTitle = sidx >= 0 ? sops[sidx].title : '';
      const sopContent = sidx >= 0 ? (sops[sidx].content || '').slice(0, 500) : '';

      return `You create image generation prompts for training videos at a KIDS CAFE (children's indoor playground).

SOP TITLE: "${sopTitle}"
NARRATION: "${narration}"

TASK: Write ONE English prompt (50-80 words) describing a SPECIFIC scene that matches this narration.

CRITICAL RULES:
- The subject is ALWAYS: "A young Korean woman in a light blue polo shirt and beige apron" (kids cafe staff)
- The setting is ALWAYS: a colorful kids cafe / indoor playground / playroom / training room
- NEVER describe the person as a doctor, nurse, scientist, or any medical professional
- NEVER include stethoscope, lab coat, white coat, or medical equipment
- Focus on the SPECIFIC ACTION described in the narration

FORMAT: "[Camera angle]. [Person in polo shirt and apron] [doing specific action matching narration]. [Kids cafe / playroom setting]. Warm bright lighting, candid photo."

EXAMPLES:
- Narration about child development → "Medium shot. A young Korean woman in a light blue polo shirt and beige apron sitting on the floor with toddlers, observing their play with building blocks. Bright colorful kids cafe playroom with foam mats. Warm lighting, candid photo."
- Narration about handwashing → "Close-up shot. A young Korean woman in a light blue polo shirt carefully washing her hands with soap at a kitchen sink. Clean kids cafe kitchen with warm lighting, candid photo."
- Narration about greeting → "Wide shot. A smiling Korean woman in a light blue polo shirt and beige apron bowing to welcome a family at a colorful kids cafe reception desk. Warm lighting, candid photo."

Output ONLY the prompt, nothing else.`;
    }

    window._genSingleImage = async function(sceneIdx, btnEl) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      const scene = sops[idx].script[sceneIdx];

      const origText = btnEl.textContent;
      btnEl.disabled = true;
      btnEl.textContent = '⏳ 생성 중...';

      try {
        let imgPrompt = _localPromptFromNarration(scene.narration);
        console.log('[Image] 로컬 프롬프트:', imgPrompt.slice(0, 80) + '...');
        try {
          const g = await callGemini(_buildImagePrompt(scene.narration));
          if (g && g.length > 20) {
            imgPrompt = g.trim().replace(/^["']|["']$/g, '');
            console.log('[Image] Gemini 업그레이드:', imgPrompt.slice(0, 80) + '...');
          }
        } catch (e) { console.warn('[Image] Gemini 실패, 로컬 사용:', e.message); }

        const imgRes = await fetch('/api/image', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'generate-multi', visual: imgPrompt, narration: scene.narration, sceneIndex: sceneIdx, totalScenes: sops[idx].script.length })
        });
        const imgData = await imgRes.json();

        if (imgData.images && imgData.images.length > 0 && imgData.images[0].imageUrl) {
          scene.imageUrl = imgData.images[0].imageUrl;
          scene.imageConfirmed = false;
          saveSops(sops);
          btnEl.disabled = false;
          btnEl.textContent = origText;
          renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
          // 렌더 후 위자드 열기
          setTimeout(() => _renderWizardScene(sceneIdx), 100);
          return;
        } else {
          alert('이미지 생성 실패. 다시 시도해주세요.');
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('Image gen failed:', e.message);
        alert('이미지 생성 실패: ' + e.message);
      }

      btnEl.disabled = false;
      btnEl.textContent = origText;
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
    }

    // ===== 이미지 일괄 사전 생성 =====
    window._generateAllImages = async function() {
      _isGeneratingImages = true;
      try {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) { _isGeneratingImages = false; return; }
      const sop = sops[idx];

      if (!sop.script || sop.script.length === 0) {
        alert('스크립트가 없습니다. 먼저 스크립트를 저장하세요.');
        return;
      }

      // 확정된 이미지는 건너뛰기
      const needGen = sop.script.filter(s => !s.imageConfirmed);
      if (needGen.length === 0) {
        alert('모든 씬의 이미지가 확정되었습니다.');
        return;
      }

      const total = needGen.length;
      if (!confirm(`${total}개 씬의 이미지를 생성합니다.\n예상 비용: ~$${(total * 0.02).toFixed(2)}\n예상 시간: ~${Math.ceil(total * 3)}초 (3개씩 병렬 생성)\n\n진행하시겠습니까?`)) return;

      // 프로그레스 바 표시
      const progressId = 'imgGenProgress';
      const area = document.getElementById('aiResultArea');
      area.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', `
        <div id="${progressId}" class="card" style="margin-bottom:16px; padding:16px;">
          <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; margin-bottom:8px;">
            <strong>🎨 이미지 생성 중...</strong>
            <span id="imgGenCount">0 / ${total}</span>
          </div>
          <div style="background:#e2e8f0; border-radius:8px; height:8px; overflow:hidden;">
            <div id="imgGenBar" style="background:linear-gradient(90deg,#6366f1,#8b5cf6); height:100%; width:0%; transition:width 0.3s;"></div>
          </div>
          <div id="imgGenStatus" style="font-size:12px; color:var(--gray-500); margin-top:6px;">이미지 병렬 생성 중...</div>
        </div>
      `);

      // 씬 인덱스 목록 (확정 안 된 것만)
      const sceneJobs = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < sop.script.length; i++) {
        if (!sop.script[i].imageConfirmed) sceneJobs.push(i);
      }

      let done = 0;
      const BATCH_SIZE = 3; // 3개씩 병렬 생성

      for (let b = 0; b < sceneJobs.length; b += BATCH_SIZE) {
        const batch = sceneJobs.slice(b, b + BATCH_SIZE);
        const statusEl = document.getElementById('imgGenStatus');
        if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = `씬 ${batch.map(i => sop.script[i].scene).join(', ')} 병렬 생성 중...`;

        // 배치 내 병렬 처리
        await Promise.all(batch.map(async (i) => {
          const scene = sop.script[i];
          try {
            // 나레이션 → 서버에서 바로 이미지 생성 (Gemini 이중 호출 제거)
            const imgRes = await fetch('/api/image', {
              method: 'POST',
              headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
              body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'generate-multi', visual: scene.visual || '', narration: scene.narration, sceneIndex: i, totalScenes: sop.script.length })
            });
            const imgData = await imgRes.json();

            if (imgData.images && imgData.images.length > 0 && imgData.images[0].imageUrl) {
              scene.imageUrl = imgData.images[0].imageUrl;
            }
          } catch (e) {
            console.warn(`씬 ${scene.scene} 이미지 생성 실패:`, e.message);
          }

          done++;
          const countEl = document.getElementById('imgGenCount');
          const barEl = document.getElementById('imgGenBar');
          if (countEl) countEl.textContent = `${done} / ${total}`;
          if (barEl) barEl.style.width = (done / total * 100) + '%';
        }));

        // 배치마다 중간 저장
        saveSops(sops);

        // 배치 간 1초 딜레이 (API 제한 방지)
        if (b + BATCH_SIZE < sceneJobs.length) {
          await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000));
        }
      }

      // 저장 (중간 저장은 5개마다)
      saveSops(sops);

      // 프로그레스 제거 후 리뷰 패널 열기
      const progressEl = document.getElementById(progressId);
      if (progressEl) progressEl.remove();

      renderAiResults(sop);
      _openSceneWizard(0); // 첫 씬부터 순차 리뷰 시작
    } finally { _isGeneratingImages = false; }
    }

    // ===== 이미지 리뷰 패널 (전체 씬 한눈에) =====
    window._openImageReview = function() {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      const sop = sops[idx];
      if (!sop.script || sop.script.length === 0) return;

      const confirmed = sop.script.filter(s => s.imageConfirmed).length;
      const generated = sop.script.filter(s => s.imageUrl).length;

      const modal = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      const overlay = document.getElementById('modalOverlay');

      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div style="padding:24px; max-width:900px; max-height:80vh; overflow-y:auto;">
          <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:20px;">
            <h3 style="margin:0;">🖼️ 이미지 리뷰 (${sop.script.length}개 씬)</h3>
            <div style="font-size:13px;">
              ✅ 확정: <strong>${confirmed}</strong> / ${sop.script.length}
              &nbsp;|&nbsp; 🖼️ 생성됨: <strong>${generated}</strong> / ${sop.script.length}
            </div>
          </div>

          ${confirmed === sop.script.length
            ? `<div style="background:#ecfdf5;padding:12px;border-radius:8px;margin-bottom:16px;color:#059669;font-weight:600;text-align:center;">🎉 모든 씬 이미지가 확정되었습니다!</div>`
            : `<div style="background:#fffbeb;padding:12px;border-radius:8px;margin-bottom:16px;color:#d97706;font-size:13px;text-align:center;">미확정 이미지는 노란 테두리로 표시됩니다. 각 이미지를 확인 후 확정해주세요.</div>`
          }

          <div style="display:grid; grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill, minmax(340px, 1fr)); gap:20px;">
            ${sop.script.map((s, i) => `
              <div style="border:3px solid ${s.imageConfirmed ? '#10b981' : s.imageUrl ? '#f59e0b' : '#d1d5db'}; border-radius:16px; overflow:hidden; background:white; box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.08);">
                <div style="aspect-ratio:16/9; background:#f1f5f9; display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:center; overflow:hidden; min-height:180px;">
                  ${s.imageUrl
                    ? `<img src="${s.imageUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;" alt="씬${s.scene}">`
                    : `<div style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-size:48px;">🎨</span><div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:14px;margin-top:8px;">이미지 없음</div></div>`
                  }
                </div>
                <div style="padding:16px;">
                  <div style="font-size:16px;color:#374151;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:6px;">씬 ${s.scene}</div>
                  <div style="font-size:14px;color:#6b7280;line-height:1.5;max-height:60px;overflow:hidden;">${s.narration.slice(0, 80)}${s.narration.length > 80 ? '...' : ''}</div>
                  <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:14px;flex-wrap:wrap;">
                    ${s.imageConfirmed
                      ? `<span style="font-size:16px;color:#10b981;font-weight:700;padding:8px 0;">✅ 확정됨</span>
                         <button onclick="_unconfirmFromReview(${i})" style="margin-left:auto;font-size:14px;padding:8px 16px;background:none;border:2px solid #ef4444;color:#ef4444;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:600;">확정 해제</button>`
                      : s.imageUrl
                        ? `<button onclick="_confirmFromReview(${i})" style="font-size:15px;padding:10px 20px;background:#10b981;color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;">✅ 확정</button>
                           <button onclick="_regenFromReview(${i})" style="font-size:15px;padding:10px 20px;background:#6366f1;color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;">🔄 재생성</button>
                           <button onclick="_removeFromReview(${i})" style="font-size:15px;padding:10px 20px;background:none;border:2px solid #ef4444;color:#ef4444;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;">🗑️</button>`
                        : `<button onclick="_regenFromReview(${i})" style="font-size:15px;padding:10px 20px;background:#6366f1;color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;width:100%;">🎨 이미지 생성</button>`
                    }
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
          </div>

          <div style="display:flex;gap:12px;margin-top:24px;justify-content:center;">
            ${confirmed < sop.script.length && generated > 0 ? `
              <button onclick="_confirmAllImages()" style="padding:14px 32px;background:#10b981;color:white;border:none;border-radius:10px;cursor:pointer;font-size:16px;font-weight:700;">✅ 전체 확정</button>
            ` : ''}
            <button onclick="closeModal()" style="padding:14px 32px;background:#6b7280;color:white;border:none;border-radius:10px;cursor:pointer;font-size:16px;font-weight:600;">닫기</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
      overlay.classList.add('show');
    }

    window._confirmFromReview = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = true;
      saveSops(sops);
      _openImageReview();
    }

    window._unconfirmFromReview = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = false;
      saveSops(sops);
      _openImageReview();
    }

    window._removeFromReview = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageUrl = null;
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = false;
      saveSops(sops);
      _openImageReview();
    }

    window._regenFromReview = async function(sceneIdx) {
      closeModal();
      _openImageManager(sceneIdx);
      setTimeout(() => _generateSceneImage(sceneIdx), 300);
    }

    window._confirmAllImages = function() {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      let count = 0;
      sops[idx].script.forEach(s => {
        if (s.imageUrl && !s.imageConfirmed) { s.imageConfirmed = true; count++; }
      });
      saveSops(sops);
      _openImageReview();
    }

    // ===== 순차 리뷰 위자드 (한 씬씩 크게 보기) =====
    window._openSceneWizard = function(startIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      const sop = sops[idx];
      if (!sop.script || sop.script.length === 0) return;

      // 이미지가 있는 첫 미확정 씬부터 시작
      let currentIdx = startIdx;
      while (currentIdx < sop.script.length && sop.script[currentIdx].imageConfirmed) {
        currentIdx++;
      }
      if (currentIdx >= sop.script.length) currentIdx = 0; // 전부 확정이면 처음부터

      _renderWizardScene(currentIdx);
    }

    window._renderWizardScene = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      const sop = sops[idx];
      const scene = sop.script[sceneIdx];
      if (!scene) return;

      const total = sop.script.length;
      const confirmed = sop.script.filter(s => s.imageConfirmed).length;

      const modal = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      const overlay = document.getElementById('modalOverlay');

      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div style="padding:24px; max-width:1100px; width:95vw;">
          <!-- 상단: 진행률 -->
          <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:16px;">
            <h3 style="margin:0; font-size:20px;">씬 ${scene.scene} / ${total}</h3>
            <div style="font-size:14px; color:#6b7280;">✅ ${confirmed} 확정 / ${total} 전체</div>
          </div>
          <div style="background:#e2e8f0; border-radius:8px; height:6px; margin-bottom:20px;">
            <div style="background:#10b981; height:100%; border-radius:8px; width:${(confirmed/total*100)}%; transition:width 0.3s;"></div>
          </div>

          <!-- 이미지 -->
          <div style="aspect-ratio:16/9; background:#f1f5f9; border-radius:12px; overflow:hidden; display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:center; margin-bottom:16px; min-height:450px; border:3px solid ${scene.imageConfirmed ? '#10b981' : scene.imageUrl ? '#f59e0b' : '#d1d5db'};">
            ${scene.imageUrl
              ? `<img src="${scene.imageUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;" alt="씬${scene.scene}">`
              : `<div style="text-align:center;"><span style="font-size:64px;">🎨</span><div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:16px;margin-top:12px;">이미지 없음</div></div>`
            }
          </div>

          <!-- 나레이션 텍스트 -->
          <div style="background:#f8fafc; border-radius:10px; padding:16px; margin-bottom:20px; border:1px solid #e2e8f0;">
            <div style="font-size:12px; color:#9ca3af; margin-bottom:4px; font-weight:600;">나레이션</div>
            <div style="font-size:15px; line-height:1.7; color:#374151;">${scene.narration}</div>
          </div>

          <!-- 액션 버튼 -->
          <div style="display:flex; gap:10px; flex-wrap:wrap; justify-content:center; margin-bottom:16px;">
            ${scene.imageUrl && !scene.imageConfirmed ? `
              <button onclick="_wizardConfirm(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:14px 28px; font-size:16px; font-weight:700; background:#10b981; color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
                ✅ 확정
              </button>
            ` : ''}
            ${scene.imageConfirmed ? `
              <button onclick="_wizardUnconfirm(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:14px 28px; font-size:16px; font-weight:700; background:none; border:2px solid #ef4444; color:#ef4444; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
                확정 해제
              </button>
            ` : ''}
            <button onclick="_wizardRegen(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:14px 28px; font-size:16px; font-weight:700; background:#6366f1; color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
              🔄 재생성
            </button>
            ${scene.imageUrl ? `
              <button onclick="_wizardRemove(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:14px 28px; font-size:16px; font-weight:700; background:none; border:2px solid #ef4444; color:#ef4444; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
                🗑️ 삭제
              </button>
            ` : ''}
          </div>

          <!-- 네비게이션 -->
          <div style="display:flex; gap:10px; justify-content:center; border-top:1px solid #e2e8f0; padding-top:16px;">
            <button onclick="_renderWizardScene(${sceneIdx > 0 ? sceneIdx - 1 : total - 1})" style="padding:12px 24px; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; background:#e2e8f0; color:#374151; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
              ◀ 이전
            </button>
            <button onclick="_renderWizardScene(${sceneIdx < total - 1 ? sceneIdx + 1 : 0})" style="padding:12px 24px; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; background:#e2e8f0; color:#374151; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
              다음 ▶
            </button>
            <button onclick="closeModal(); renderAiResults(getSops().find(s=>s.id===currentSopId));" style="padding:12px 24px; font-size:15px; font-weight:600; background:#6b7280; color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;">
              닫기
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
      overlay.classList.add('show');
    }

    window._wizardConfirm = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = true;
      saveSops(sops);
      // 다음 미확정 씬으로 이동
      let next = sceneIdx + 1;
      while (next < sops[idx].script.length && sops[idx].script[next].imageConfirmed) next++;
      if (next >= sops[idx].script.length) {
        // 전부 확정됨
        const allConfirmed = sops[idx].script.every(s => s.imageConfirmed);
        if (allConfirmed) {
          closeModal();
          renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
          alert('🎉 모든 씬 이미지가 확정되었습니다!');
          return;
        }
        next = 0;
      }
      _renderWizardScene(next);
    }

    window._wizardUnconfirm = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = false;
      saveSops(sops);
      _renderWizardScene(sceneIdx);
    }

    window._wizardRegen = async function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      const scene = sops[idx].script[sceneIdx];

      // 이미지 영역에 로딩 표시
      const modal = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      const imgArea = modal.querySelector('[style*="aspect-ratio"]');
      if (imgArea) imgArea.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;"><div style="font-size:48px;">⏳</div><div style="color:#6b7280;font-size:16px;margin-top:12px;">이미지 생성 중...</div></div>`;

      try {
        let imgPrompt = _localPromptFromNarration(scene.narration);
        console.log('[Image] 로컬 프롬프트:', imgPrompt.slice(0, 80) + '...');
        try {
          const g = await callGemini(_buildImagePrompt(scene.narration));
          if (g && g.length > 20) {
            imgPrompt = g.trim().replace(/^["']|["']$/g, '');
            console.log('[Image] Gemini 업그레이드:', imgPrompt.slice(0, 80) + '...');
          }
        } catch (e) { console.warn('[Image] Gemini 실패, 로컬 사용:', e.message); }

        const imgRes = await fetch('/api/image', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'generate-multi', visual: imgPrompt, narration: scene.narration, sceneIndex: sceneIdx, totalScenes: sops[idx].script.length })
        });
        const imgData = await imgRes.json();

        if (imgData.images && imgData.images.length > 0 && imgData.images[0].imageUrl) {
          scene.imageUrl = imgData.images[0].imageUrl;
          scene.imageConfirmed = false;
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('Image regen failed:', e.message);
        alert('이미지 생성 실패: ' + e.message);
      }

      saveSops(sops);
      _renderWizardScene(sceneIdx);
    }

    window._wizardRemove = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageUrl = null;
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = false;
      saveSops(sops);
      _renderWizardScene(sceneIdx);
    }

    // ===== 씬별 이미지 관리 팝업 =====
    window._openImageManager = function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      const scene = sops[idx].script[sceneIdx];
      if (!scene) return;

      // textarea에서 최신 나레이션 반영
      const ta = document.querySelector(`.scene-narration[data-index="${sceneIdx}"]`);
      if (ta) scene.narration = ta.value.trim();

      const modal = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      const overlay = document.getElementById('modalOverlay');

      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div style="padding:24px; max-width:600px;">
          <h3 style="margin-bottom:16px;">🎨 씬 ${scene.scene} 이미지 관리</h3>
          <div style="background:#f8fafc; padding:12px; border-radius:8px; margin-bottom:16px; font-size:13px; color:var(--gray-600); line-height:1.6; max-height:100px; overflow-y:auto;">
            ${scene.narration.slice(0, 200)}${scene.narration.length > 200 ? '...' : ''}
          </div>
          <div id="imgManagerPreview" style="width:100%; aspect-ratio:16/9; background:#e2e8f0; border-radius:12px; display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:center; margin-bottom:16px; overflow:hidden;">
            ${scene.imageUrl
              ? `<img src="${scene.imageUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;" alt="씬${scene.scene}">`
              : `<span style="color:#94a3b8; font-size:14px;">이미지 없음</span>`
            }
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex; gap:8px; flex-wrap:wrap;">
            <button id="imgGenBtn" onclick="_generateSceneImage(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:10px 20px; background:linear-gradient(135deg,#6366f1,#8b5cf6); color:white; border:none; border-radius:8px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">
              ${scene.imageUrl ? '🔄 새로 생성' : '🎨 이미지 생성'}
            </button>
            ${scene.imageUrl ? `
              <button onclick="_confirmSceneImage(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:10px 20px; background:var(--success); color:white; border:none; border-radius:8px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px; font-weight:600;">
                ✅ 이 이미지로 확정
              </button>
              <button onclick="_removeSceneImage(${sceneIdx})" style="padding:10px 20px; background:none; color:#e55; border:1px solid #e55; border-radius:8px; cursor:pointer; font-size:13px;">
                🗑️ 삭제
              </button>
            ` : ''}
          </div>
          <div id="imgGenMsg" style="margin-top:12px; font-size:12px; color:var(--gray-500);"></div>
        </div>
      `;
      overlay.classList.add('show');
    }

    window._generateSceneImage = async function(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;
      const scene = sops[idx].script[sceneIdx];

      const btn = document.getElementById('imgGenBtn');
      const msg = document.getElementById('imgGenMsg');
      const preview = document.getElementById('imgManagerPreview');
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = '⏳ 생성 중...'; }
      if (msg) msg.textContent = 'Gemini로 프롬프트 변환 → FLUX 이미지 생성 중... (10~15초)';

      try {
        // 1) Gemini → 영어 이미지 프롬프트
