        let imgPrompt = 'A professional Korean staff member in a bright, clean modern workplace. Warm natural lighting, educational training scene.';
        try {
          const gen = await callGemini(_buildImagePrompt(scene.narration));
          if (gen && gen.length > 20) imgPrompt = gen.trim();
          if (msg) msg.textContent = '이미지 생성 중...';
        } catch (e) {}

        // 2) FLUX 이미지 생성
        const imgRes = await fetch('/api/image', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'generate-multi', visual: imgPrompt, narration: scene.narration, sceneIndex: sceneIdx, totalScenes: sops[idx].script.length })
        });
        const imgData = await imgRes.json();

        if (imgData.images && imgData.images[0]?.imageUrl) {
          scene.imageUrl = imgData.images[0].imageUrl;
          saveSops(sops);

          // 미리보기 업데이트
          if (preview) preview.innerHTML = `<img src="${scene.imageUrl}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;" alt="씬${scene.scene}">`;
          if (msg) msg.innerHTML = `<span style="color:var(--success);">✅ 생성 완료! 마음에 들면 "확정", 아니면 "새로 생성"을 눌러주세요.</span>`;
          if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '🔄 새로 생성'; }

          // 팝업 버튼 영역 업데이트 (확정/삭제 추가)
          _openImageManager(sceneIdx);
        } else {
          if (msg) msg.innerHTML = `<span style="color:#e55;">❌ 생성 실패. 다시 시도해주세요.</span>`;
          if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '🎨 다시 시도'; }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        if (msg) msg.innerHTML = `<span style="color:#e55;">❌ 오류: ${e.message}</span>`;
        if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '🎨 다시 시도'; }
      }
    }

    function _confirmSceneImage(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = true;
      saveSops(sops);
      closeModal();
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
    }

    function _removeSceneImage(sceneIdx) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageUrl = null;
      sops[idx].script[sceneIdx].imageConfirmed = false;
      saveSops(sops);
      _openImageManager(sceneIdx);
    }

    window._addScene = function() {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      if (!sops[idx].script) sops[idx].script = [];
      sops[idx].script.push({ scene: sops[idx].script.length + 1, narration: '', visual: 'New scene' });
      saveSops(sops);
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);

      // 새 씬으로 스크롤
      setTimeout(() => {
        const editor = document.getElementById('scriptEditor');
        if (editor) editor.lastElementChild.querySelector('textarea').focus();
      }, 100);
    }

    window._deleteScene = function(index) {
      if (!confirm(`씬 ${index + 1}을 삭제하시겠습니까?`)) return;
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      sops[idx].script.splice(index, 1);
      sops[idx].script.forEach((s, i) => s.scene = i + 1);
      saveSops(sops);
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
    }

    window._moveScene = function(index, direction) {
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      const newIdx = index + direction;
      if (newIdx < 0 || newIdx >= sops[idx].script.length) return;

      // 현재 textarea 값을 먼저 반영
      const textareas = document.querySelectorAll('.scene-narration');
      textareas.forEach((ta, i) => { sops[idx].script[i].narration = ta.value; });

      const temp = sops[idx].script[index];
      sops[idx].script[index] = sops[idx].script[newIdx];
      sops[idx].script[newIdx] = temp;
      sops[idx].script.forEach((s, i) => s.scene = i + 1);
      saveSops(sops);
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);
    }

    // ===== AI 결과 렌더링 =====
    function renderAiResults(sop) {
      const area = document.getElementById('aiResultArea');

      if (!sop.script || sop.script.length === 0) {
        area.innerHTML = '';
        return;
      }

      let html = '';

      // 스크립트 편집기
      html += `
        <div class="ai-result-section" style="margin-top:24px;">
          <div class="ai-result-header" style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; flex-wrap:wrap; gap:8px;">
            <h4 style="font-size:18px;">&#127910; 슬라이드 스크립트 (${sop.script.length}개 씬)</h4>
            <span style="font-size:14px; color:var(--gray-500);">예상 ${Math.round(sop.script.length * 0.7)}분</span>
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex; gap:10px; flex-wrap:wrap; margin:12px 0 16px;">
            <button style="padding:12px 20px; font-size:15px; font-weight:700; background:#6366f1; color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;" onclick="_addScene()">➕ 씬 추가</button>
            <button style="padding:12px 20px; font-size:15px; font-weight:700; background:#3b82f6; color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;" onclick="_saveScripts()">💾 스크립트 저장</button>
            <button style="padding:12px 20px; font-size:15px; font-weight:700; background:linear-gradient(135deg,#f59e0b,#ef4444); color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;" onclick="_generateAllImages()">🎨 이미지 일괄 생성</button>
            <button style="padding:12px 20px; font-size:15px; font-weight:700; background:#10b981; color:white; border:none; border-radius:10px; cursor:pointer;" onclick="_openImageReview()">🖼️ 이미지 리뷰</button>
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex; gap:12px; margin-bottom:12px; padding:10px 16px; background:#f8fafc; border-radius:8px; font-size:14px; color:var(--gray-600);">
            ✅ 확정: <strong>${sop.script.filter(x => x.imageConfirmed).length}</strong> / ${sop.script.length}
            &nbsp;&nbsp;|&nbsp;&nbsp;
            🖼️ 생성됨: <strong>${sop.script.filter(x => x.imageUrl).length}</strong> / ${sop.script.length}
          </div>
          <div class="ai-result-body" id="scriptEditor">
            ${sop.script.map((s, i) => `
              <div class="script-scene" style="position:relative; padding:12px; margin-bottom:8px; border:1px solid #e2e8f0; border-radius:10px; background:white;" data-index="${i}">
                <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:8px;">
                  <div style="font-size:16px; font-weight:700; color:#374151;">씬 ${s.scene}</div>
                  <div style="display:flex; gap:6px; align-items:center;">
                    <button onclick="_genSingleImage(${i}, this)" style="background:#6366f1;color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;padding:8px 14px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">🎨 생성</button>
                    ${s.imageUrl ? `<button onclick="_renderWizardScene(${i})" style="background:${s.imageConfirmed ? '#10b981' : '#f59e0b'};color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;padding:8px 14px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">${s.imageConfirmed ? '✅ 확정됨' : '🖼️ 보기'}</button>` : ''}
                    ${i > 0 ? `<button onclick="_moveScene(${i},-1)" style="background:none;border:2px solid #d1d5db;border-radius:8px;padding:6px 10px;cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;" title="위로">▲</button>` : ''}
                    ${i < sop.script.length - 1 ? `<button onclick="_moveScene(${i},1)" style="background:none;border:2px solid #d1d5db;border-radius:8px;padding:6px 10px;cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;" title="아래로">▼</button>` : ''}
                    <button onclick="_deleteScene(${i})" style="background:none;border:2px solid #ef4444;color:#ef4444;border-radius:8px;padding:6px 10px;cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;font-weight:700;" title="삭제">✕</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <textarea class="scene-narration" data-index="${i}" rows="3" style="width:100%;border:2px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;padding:10px;font-size:14px;line-height:1.7;resize:vertical;font-family:inherit;">${s.narration}</textarea>
              </div>
            `).join('')}
          </div>
        </div>`;

      // 퀴즈 프리뷰
      if (sop.quizzes && sop.quizzes.length > 0) {
        html += `
          <div class="ai-result-section" style="margin-top:16px;">
            <div class="ai-result-header">
              <h4>&#10067; AI 생성 퀴즈 (${sop.quizzes.length}문제)</h4>
            </div>
            <div class="ai-result-body">
              ${sop.quizzes.map((q, i) => `
                <div class="quiz-preview-item">
                  <div class="q-text">Q${i + 1}. ${q.question}</div>
                  <div class="q-options">
                    ${q.options.map((o, oi) => `<span class="q-opt ${oi === q.correct ? 'correct' : 'wrong'}">${o}</span>`).join('')}
                  </div>
                </div>
              `).join('')}
            </div>
          </div>`;
      }

      // 액션 버튼
      const isPublished = sop.status === 'published';
      const videoEnabled = AI_CONFIG.videoProvider !== 'none';
      html += `
        <div style="display:flex; gap:8px; margin-top:20px; flex-wrap:wrap;">
          <button class="btn" style="padding:12px 24px; background:linear-gradient(135deg,#6366f1,#8b5cf6); color:white; border:none; border-radius:8px; cursor:pointer; font-size:14px; font-weight:600;" onclick="SlidePlayer.open('${sop.id}')">
            &#9654; 슬라이드 미리보기
          </button>
          ${!isPublished ? `
            <button class="btn btn-success" style="padding:12px 24px;" onclick="publishSop()">
              &#9989; 검토 완료 → 직원에게 배포
            </button>
          ` : `
            <div style="display:flex; gap:8px; align-items:center; flex:1;">
              <div class="alert alert-success" style="flex:1; margin:0;">
                &#9989; 배포됨
              </div>
              <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:10px 18px; font-size:13px; color:#f59e0b; border-color:#f59e0b;" onclick="unpublishSop()">
                &#9998; 수정모드로 전환
              </button>
              <button class="btn btn-success" style="padding:10px 18px; font-size:13px;" onclick="publishSop()">
                &#128260; 재배포
              </button>
            </div>
          `}
          <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:12px 24px;" onclick="generateContent()">
            &#128260; 스크립트/퀴즈 다시 생성
          </button>
          ${videoEnabled ? `
            <button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:12px 24px; background:#7c3aed;" onclick="generateSopVideos()">
              &#127910; AI 영상 생성 (${sop.script.length}씬)
            </button>
          ` : `
            <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:12px 24px; font-size:13px;" onclick="showPage('settings')">
              &#127910; 영상 생성하려면 → AI 설정
            </button>
          `}
        </div>`;

      area.innerHTML = html;
    }

    // ===== 수정모드 전환 (배포 해제) =====
    function unpublishSop() {
      if (!hasPermission('sop_edit')) { alert('권한이 없습니다.'); return; }
      if (!currentSopId) return;
      if (!confirm('배포를 해제하고 수정모드로 전환합니다.\n직원들은 이 SOP를 더 이상 볼 수 없습니다.\n계속하시겠습니까?')) return;

      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      sops[idx].status = 'draft';
      saveSops(sops);
      AuditLog.add('publish', 'unpublish', `배포 해제: "${sops[idx].title}"`);
      renderStatusFlow('draft');
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);

      alert('✏️ 수정모드로 전환되었습니다. 스크립트를 수정한 후 재배포하세요.');
    }

    // ===== 배포 =====
    function publishSop() {
      if (!hasPermission('sop_edit')) { alert('SOP 배포 권한이 없습니다.'); return; }
      if (!currentSopId) return;
      const sops = getSops();
      const idx = sops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (idx === -1) return;

      // 배포 전 검증
      if (!sops[idx].script || sops[idx].script.length === 0) {
        alert('⚠️ 스크립트가 없습니다. 먼저 스크립트를 생성하세요.');
        return;
      }
      if (!sops[idx].quizzes || sops[idx].quizzes.length === 0) {
        if (!confirm('퀴즈가 없습니다. 퀴즈 없이 배포하시겠습니까?')) return;
      }

      sops[idx].status = 'published';
      saveSops(sops);
      AuditLog.add('publish', 'publish', `SOP 배포: "${sops[idx].title}"`);
      renderStatusFlow('published');
      renderAiResults(sops[idx]);

      // 성공 알림
      const area = document.getElementById('aiResultArea');
      area.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', `
        <div class="alert alert-success" style="margin-bottom:16px; font-size:15px; font-weight:600;">
          &#127881; 배포 완료! 직원들이 이제 이 교육을 학습할 수 있습니다.
        </div>
      `);
    }

    // ===== 생성된 콘텐츠 목록 =====
    function renderGeneratedContent() {
      const sops = getSops().filter(s => s.script && s.script.length > 0);
      const container = document.getElementById('generatedContentList');

      if (sops.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--gray-500); text-align:center; padding:40px;">아직 생성된 콘텐츠가 없습니다. SOP를 작성하고 AI 생성을 실행해보세요.</p>';
        return;
      }

      container.innerHTML = sops.map(sop => {
        const statusMap = {
          generated: { label: '검토 필요', color: 'var(--warning)', bg: '#fef3c7' },
          reviewed: { label: '검토 완료', color: 'var(--primary)', bg: 'var(--primary-light)' },
          published: { label: '배포됨', color: 'var(--success)', bg: '#dcfce7' },
        };
        const st = statusMap[sop.status] || statusMap.generated;

        return `
          <div class="card" style="margin-bottom:16px;">
            <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:start; margin-bottom:12px;">
              <div>
                <h4 style="font-size:16px;">${sop.title}</h4>
                <p style="font-size:13px; color:var(--gray-500);">${sop.category} · 스크립트 ${sop.script.length}씬 · 퀴즈 ${sop.quizzes?.length || 0}문제</p>
              </div>
              <span class="badge" style="background:${st.bg}; color:${st.color};">${st.label}</span>
            </div>
            <div style="display:flex; gap:8px;">
              <button class="btn" style="padding:6px 14px; font-size:13px; background:linear-gradient(135deg,#6366f1,#8b5cf6); color:white; border:none; border-radius:8px; cursor:pointer;" onclick="SlidePlayer.open('${sop.id}')">&#9654; 미리보기</button>
              <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:6px 14px; font-size:13px;" onclick="showPage('sop'); setTimeout(() => openSopEditor('${sop.id}'), 100);">상세 보기</button>
              ${sop.status !== 'published' ? `<button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:6px 14px; font-size:13px;" onclick="currentSopId='${sop.id}'; publishSop(); renderGeneratedContent();">배포하기</button>` : ''}
            </div>
          </div>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    // ===== 대시보드 (실데이터) =====
    function getEmployeesWithProgress() {
      const all = Progress.getAllEmployeesProgress();
      return getFilteredEmployees(all);
    }

    function renderDashboard() {
      checkDeadlineAlerts();
      const emps = getEmployeesWithProgress();
      const c = emps.filter(e => e.status === 'completed').length;
      const p = emps.filter(e => e.status === 'in_progress').length;
      const n = emps.filter(e => e.status === 'not_started').length;
      document.getElementById('statTotalEmp').textContent = emps.length;
      document.getElementById('statCompleted').textContent = c;
      document.getElementById('statInProgress').textContent = p;
      document.getElementById('statNotStarted').textContent = n;
      renderEmployeeTable(emps);

      // 지점 필터 드롭다운 채우기
      const branchFilter = document.getElementById('branchFilter');
      if (branchFilter) {
        if (adminRole === 'branch_manager') {
          branchFilter.innerHTML = '<option value="' + adminBranch + '">' + adminBranch + '</option>';
          branchFilter.disabled = true;
        } else {
          const prev = branchFilter.value;
          const branchNames = [...new Set(emps.map(e => e.branch).filter(Boolean))].sort();
          branchFilter.innerHTML = '<option value="">전체 지점</option>' +
            branchNames.map(b => `<option value="${b}"${b===prev?' selected':''}>${b}</option>`).join('');
        }
      }

      // 상태 분포 바 차트
      const total = emps.length || 1;
      const statusChart = document.getElementById('statusChart');
      if (statusChart) {
        statusChart.innerHTML = [
          { label: '완료', val: c, color: 'var(--success)' },
          { label: '진행중', val: p, color: 'var(--warning)' },
          { label: '미시작', val: n, color: 'var(--danger)' },
        ].map(s => `<div style="flex:1;text-align:center;">
          <div style="background:${s.color};width:100%;height:${Math.max((s.val/total)*100, 5)}%;border-radius:6px 6px 0 0;min-height:8px;transition:height 0.3s;"></div>
          <div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:700;margin-top:8px;">${s.val}</div>
          <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--gray-500);">${s.label}</div>
        </div>`).join('');
      }

      // 지점별 진행률 차트
      const branches = {};
      emps.forEach(e => {
        if (!branches[e.branch]) branches[e.branch] = { sum: 0, count: 0 };
        branches[e.branch].sum += e.progress;
        branches[e.branch].count++;
      });
      const branchChart = document.getElementById('branchChart');
      if (branchChart) {
        branchChart.innerHTML = Object.entries(branches).map(([name, d]) => {
          const avg = Math.round(d.sum / d.count);
          return `<div>
            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:2px;">
              <span>${name}</span><span style="font-weight:600;">${avg}%</span>
            </div>
            <div class="progress-bar" style="height:6px;"><div class="fill ${avg>=100?'success':''}" style="width:${avg}%"></div></div>
          </div>`;
        }).join('');
      }
    }

    function renderEmployeeTable(employees) {
      document.getElementById('empTableBody').innerHTML = employees.map(emp => {
        const badge = emp.status === 'completed' ? '<span class="badge badge-success">완료</span>'
          : emp.status === 'in_progress' ? '<span class="badge badge-warning">진행중</span>'
          : '<span class="badge badge-danger">미시작</span>';
        const last = emp.lastActive ? formatDate(emp.lastActive) : '-';
        return `<tr style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="showEmployeeDetail('${emp.id}')">
          <td><strong>${emp.name}</strong></td><td style="font-size:13px;">${emp.branch}</td>
          <td><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;"><div class="progress-bar" style="width:80px;"><div class="fill ${emp.progress>=100?'success':''}" style="width:${emp.progress}%"></div></div><span style="font-size:13px;">${emp.progress}%</span></div></td>
          <td style="font-size:13px;">${emp.avgScore?emp.avgScore+'점':'-'}</td><td style="font-size:13px;color:var(--gray-500);">${last}</td><td>${badge}</td></tr>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    function filterEmployees() {
      const q = document.getElementById('empSearch').value.toLowerCase();
      const branch = document.getElementById('branchFilter')?.value || '';
      const emps = getEmployeesWithProgress();
      const filtered = emps.filter(e => {
        const matchBranch = !branch || e.branch === branch;
        const matchSearch = !q || e.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) || e.branch.toLowerCase().includes(q);
        return matchBranch && matchSearch;
      });
      renderEmployeeTable(filtered);
      // 요약 통계 업데이트
      document.getElementById('statTotalEmp').textContent = filtered.length;
      document.getElementById('statCompleted').textContent = filtered.filter(e => e.status === 'completed').length;
      document.getElementById('statInProgress').textContent = filtered.filter(e => e.status === 'in_progress').length;
      document.getElementById('statNotStarted').textContent = filtered.filter(e => e.status === 'not_started').length;
    }

    // ===== 직원 상세 (클릭 시 모달) =====
    function showEmployeeDetail(empId) {
      const emp = EmployeeStore.getById(empId);
      const prog = Progress.getEmployeeProgress(empId);
      if (!emp) return;

      const chapters = SopStore.getChapters();
      const badge = prog.status === 'completed' ? '<span class="badge badge-success">완료</span>'
        : prog.status === 'in_progress' ? '<span class="badge badge-warning">진행중</span>'
        : '<span class="badge badge-danger">미시작</span>';

      let chaptersHTML = chapters.map((ch, i) => {
        const videos = SopStore.getVideos(ch.id);
        const result = prog.chapterResults[ch.id];
        const passed = result?.passed === true;
        const videoDone = videos.filter(v => prog.completedVideoIds.includes(v.id)).length;

        let statusText = '미시작';
        let statusColor = 'var(--gray-500)';
        if (passed) { statusText = `통과 (${result.score}점)`; statusColor = 'var(--success)'; }
        else if (videoDone > 0) { statusText = `${videoDone}/${videos.length} 시청`; statusColor = 'var(--warning)'; }

        return `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100);">
          <div><strong style="font-size:14px;">${i+1}. ${ch.title}</strong>
            <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);">${videos.length}개 씬</div></div>
          <span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:${statusColor};">${statusText}</span>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');

      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      m.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:start;margin-bottom:20px;">
          <div>
            <h3 style="margin-bottom:4px;">${emp.name}</h3>
            <p style="font-size:14px;color:var(--gray-500);">${emp.email} · ${emp.branch}</p>
          </div>
          ${badge}
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:12px;margin-bottom:20px;">
          <div style="text-align:center;padding:16px;background:var(--gray-50);border-radius:8px;">
            <div style="font-size:24px;font-weight:700;color:var(--primary);">${prog.progress}%</div>
            <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);">진행률</div>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align:center;padding:16px;background:var(--gray-50);border-radius:8px;">
            <div style="font-size:24px;font-weight:700;color:var(--success);">${prog.passedChapters}/${prog.totalChapters}</div>
            <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);">통과 챕터</div>
          </div>
          <div style="text-align:center;padding:16px;background:var(--gray-50);border-radius:8px;">
            <div style="font-size:24px;font-weight:700;">${prog.avgScore || '-'}</div>
            <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);">평균 점수</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h4 style="font-size:15px;margin-bottom:8px;">챕터별 상세</h4>
        ${chaptersHTML}
        <p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);margin-top:12px;">최근 활동: ${prog.lastActive ? new Date(prog.lastActive).toLocaleString('ko-KR') : '없음'}</p>
        <button class="btn btn-outline" style="width:100%;margin-top:16px;" onclick="closeModal()">닫기</button>
      `;
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
    }

    // ===== 직원 관리 =====
    function renderEmployeeManage() {
      const emps = getEmployeesWithProgress();
      document.getElementById('empManageBody').innerHTML = emps.map(emp => {
        const mbtiData = getEmployeeMbti(emp.email);
        const mbtiHtml = mbtiData
          ? `<span class="badge" style="background:#ede9fe;color:#7c3aed;cursor:pointer;font-weight:700;" onclick="event.stopPropagation();showMbtiDetail('${emp.name}','${emp.email}')">${mbtiData.type}</span>`
          : `<span class="badge" style="background:var(--gray-100);color:var(--gray-500);">미응시</span>`;
        const gradeInfo = getEmployeeGrade(emp.email);
        const gradeHtml = gradeInfo
          ? `<span class="badge" style="background:${gradeInfo.bg};color:${gradeInfo.color};font-weight:700;">${gradeInfo.grade}</span>`
          : `<span style="color:var(--gray-400);">-</span>`;
        return `<tr><td><strong>${emp.name}</strong></td><td style="font-size:13px;">${emp.email}</td><td style="font-size:13px;">${emp.branch}</td>
        <td><span class="badge" style="background:${emp.role==='branch_manager'?'var(--primary-light)':'var(--gray-100)'}; color:${emp.role==='branch_manager'?'var(--primary)':'var(--gray-700)'};">${emp.role==='branch_manager'?'지점장':'직원'}</span></td>
        <td>${mbtiHtml}</td>
        <td>${gradeHtml}</td>
        <td style="font-size:13px;color:var(--gray-500);">${emp.created}</td>
        <td><button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:4px 12px;font-size:12px;" onclick="showEmployeeDetail('${emp.id}')">상세</button></td></tr>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    // ===== 리포트 (실데이터) =====
    function renderReports() {
      const emps = getEmployeesWithProgress();
      const branches = {};
      emps.forEach(e => {
        if (!branches[e.branch]) branches[e.branch] = {total:0,completed:0,avg:0};
        branches[e.branch].total++;
        if (e.status==='completed') branches[e.branch].completed++;
        branches[e.branch].avg += e.progress;
      });
      document.getElementById('branchReport').innerHTML = Object.entries(branches).map(([n,d]) => {
        const a = Math.round(d.avg/d.total);
        return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:16px;padding:12px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100);">
          <div style="width:140px;font-weight:600;font-size:14px;">${n}</div>
          <div style="flex:1;"><div class="progress-bar"><div class="fill ${a>=100?'success':''}" style="width:${a}%"></div></div></div>
          <div style="width:50px;text-align:right;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;">${a}%</div>
          <div style="width:80px;text-align:right;font-size:13px;color:var(--gray-500);">${d.completed}/${d.total}명</div></div>`;
      }).join('');

      // 챕터별 통과율 (실데이터)
      const chapters = SopStore.getChapters();
      document.getElementById('chapterReport').innerHTML = chapters.length > 0
        ? chapters.map((ch, i) => {
          const passCount = emps.filter(e => Progress.getEmployeeProgress(e.id).chapterResults[ch.id]?.passed).length;
          const rate = emps.length > 0 ? Math.round((passCount / emps.length) * 100) : 0;
          return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:16px;padding:12px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100);">
            <div style="width:180px;font-size:14px;"><strong>${i+1}.</strong> ${ch.title}</div>
            <div style="flex:1;"><div class="progress-bar"><div class="fill ${rate>=80?'success':''}" style="width:${rate}%"></div></div></div>
            <div style="width:50px;text-align:right;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;">${rate}%</div>
            <div style="width:60px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);">${passCount}/${emps.length}명</div></div>`;
        }).join('')
        : '<p style="color:var(--gray-500);">배포된 SOP가 없습니다</p>';
    }

    // ===== 모달/CSV =====
    function openModal(type) {
      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      if (type==='addEmployee') {
        m.innerHTML=`<h3>직원 추가</h3>
          <div class="form-group"><label>이름</label><input type="text" id="newEmpName" placeholder="홍길동"></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>이메일</label><input type="email" id="newEmpEmail" placeholder="name@company.com"></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>지점</label><select id="newEmpBranch" ${adminRole==='branch_manager'?'disabled':''}>${adminRole==='branch_manager'?'<option>'+adminBranch+'</option>':'<option>서울 강남점</option><option>서울 홍대점</option><option>부산 해운대점</option><option>호치민 1호점</option><option>하노이 1호점</option>'}</select></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>역할</label><select id="newEmpRole" ${adminRole==='branch_manager'?'disabled':''}>${adminRole==='branch_manager'?'<option value="staff">직원</option>':'<option value="staff">직원</option><option value="branch_manager">지점장</option>'}</select></div>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:24px;">
            <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="addEmployee()">추가</button>
            <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal()">취소</button>
          </div>
          <hr style="margin:24px 0;border:none;border-top:1px solid var(--gray-200);">
          <h4 style="font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px;">CSV 일괄 등록</h4>
          <p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--gray-500);margin-bottom:12px;">형식: <code>이름,이메일,지점,역할</code></p>
          <textarea id="csvInput" rows="5" style="width:100%;padding:12px;border:1px solid var(--gray-300);border-radius:8px;font-family:monospace;font-size:13px;" placeholder="홍길동,hong@co.com,서울 강남점,staff&#10;Nguyen A,nguyen@co.com,호치민 1호점,staff"></textarea>
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="margin-top:8px;width:100%;" onclick="bulkAddEmployees()">일괄 등록</button>`;
      }
      else if (type==='inviteLink') {
  const code = 'INV-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2,8).toUpperCase();
  const baseUrl = window.location.origin || 'https://your-domain.vercel.app';
  const link = baseUrl + '/register.html?code=' + code;
  m.innerHTML=`<h3>🔗 직원 초대 링크 생성</h3>
    <p style="font-size:14px;color:var(--gray-500);margin-bottom:16px;">이 링크를 직원에게 공유하면 스스로 가입할 수 있습니다</p>
    <div class="form-group"><label>지점 지정</label>
      <select id="inviteBranch" ${adminRole==='branch_manager'?'disabled':''}>${adminRole==='branch_manager'?'<option>'+adminBranch+'</option>':'<option>서울 강남점</option><option>서울 홍대점</option><option>부산 해운대점</option><option>호치민 1호점</option><option>하노이 1호점</option>'}</select></div>
    <div class="form-group"><label>최대 사용 횟수</label>
      <select id="inviteMax"><option value="5">5명</option><option value="10" selected>10명</option><option value="20">20명</option><option value="50">50명</option></select></div>
    <div class="form-group"><label>만료일</label>
      <input type="date" id="inviteExpiry" value="${new Date(Date.now()+7*24*60*60*1000).toISOString().slice(0,10)}" min="${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}">
      <span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--gray-400);">미지정 시 7일 후 만료</span></div>
    <div style="background:var(--gray-50);padding:16px;border-radius:8px;margin:16px 0;">
      <label style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);display:block;margin-bottom:4px;">초대 링크</label>
      <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;">
        <input type="text" id="inviteLinkUrl" value="${link}" readonly style="flex:1;padding:10px;border:1px solid var(--gray-300);border-radius:8px;font-size:13px;font-family:monospace;">
        <button class="btn btn-primary" style="padding:10px 16px;white-space:nowrap;" onclick="copyInviteLink()">복사</button>
      </div>
    </div>
    <p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);">⚠️ 이 링크로 가입한 직원은 자동으로 선택한 지점에 배정됩니다</p>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:20px;">
      <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="saveInvitation('${code}')">링크 활성화</button>
      <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal()">닫기</button>
    </div>`;
}
      else if (type==='sendNotification') {
        const emps = EmployeeStore.getAll();
        const empOptions = emps.map(e => `<option value="${e.email}">${e.name} (${e.email})</option>`).join('');
        m.innerHTML=`<h3>&#128227; 학습 리마인더 보내기</h3>
          <div class="form-group"><label>대상</label>
            <select id="notifTarget" onchange="document.getElementById('notifSpecificWrap').style.display=this.value==='specific'?'block':'none'">
              <option value="all">전체 직원</option>
              <option value="incomplete">미학습자만</option>
              <option value="specific">특정 직원</option>
            </select></div>
          <div id="notifSpecificWrap" style="display:none;" class="form-group"><label>직원 선택</label>
            <select id="notifSpecificEmps" multiple style="height:100px;">${empOptions}</select>
            <span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--gray-400);">Ctrl/Cmd 클릭으로 여러 명 선택</span></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>알림 유형</label>
            <select id="notifType">
              <option value="reminder">학습 리마인더</option>
              <option value="deadline">마감일 알림</option>
              <option value="newSop">새 SOP 알림</option>
              <option value="custom">관리자 메시지</option>
            </select></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>메시지</label>
            <textarea id="notifMessage" rows="3" style="width:100%;padding:12px;border:1px solid var(--gray-300);border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;">학습을 시작해주세요!</textarea></div>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:20px;">
            <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="sendNotification()">보내기</button>
            <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal()">취소</button>
          </div>`;
      }
      else if (type==='setDeadline') {
        const sops = getSops().filter(s => s.status === 'published');
        const sopOptions = sops.map(s => `<option value="${s.id}">${s.title}</option>`).join('');
        m.innerHTML=`<h3>⏰ 학습 마감일 설정</h3>
          <p style="font-size:14px;color:var(--gray-500);margin-bottom:16px;">배포된 SOP에 학습 마감일을 설정합니다</p>
          <div class="form-group"><label>대상 SOP</label>
            <select id="deadlineSop">${sopOptions || '<option disabled>배포된 SOP가 없습니다</option>'}</select></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>대상 지점</label>
            <select id="deadlineBranch"><option value="all">전체 지점</option><option>서울 강남점</option><option>서울 홍대점</option><option>부산 해운대점</option><option>호치민 1호점</option><option>하노이 1호점</option></select></div>
          <div class="form-group"><label>마감일</label>
            <input type="date" id="deadlineDate" min="${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}"></div>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:20px;">
            <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="saveDeadline()">마감일 설정</button>
            <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal()">취소</button>
          </div>
          <div id="existingDeadlines" style="margin-top:20px;"></div>`;
        renderExistingDeadlines();
      }
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
    }

    function bulkAddEmployees() {
      const csv = document.getElementById('csvInput').value.trim();
      if (!csv) { alert('CSV 데이터를 입력하세요'); return; }
      const emps = EmployeeStore.getAll();
      let added = 0;
      csv.split('\n').filter(l => l.trim()).forEach(line => {
        const [name, email, branch, role] = line.split(',').map(s => s.trim());
        if (name && email && !emps.find(e => e.email === email)) {
          emps.push({ id: 'emp-' + Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6), name, email, branch: branch || '미지정', role: role || 'staff', created: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10) });
          added++;
        }
      });
      EmployeeStore.save(emps);
      AuditLog.add('employee', 'bulk_add', `직원 ${added}명 일괄 등록`);
      closeModal();
      renderEmployeeManage();
      alert(added + '명의 직원이 등록되었습니다.');
    }

    function addEmployee() {
      const name = document.getElementById('newEmpName').value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('newEmpEmail').value.trim();
      const branch = document.getElementById('newEmpBranch').value;
      const role = document.getElementById('newEmpRole').value;
      if (!name || !email) { alert('이름과 이메일을 입력하세요'); return; }

      const emps = EmployeeStore.getAll();
      if (emps.find(e => e.email === email)) { alert('이미 등록된 이메일입니다'); return; }
      emps.push({
        id: 'emp-' + Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6),
        name, email, branch, role,
        created: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)
      });
      EmployeeStore.save(emps);

      AuditLog.add('employee', 'add', `직원 추가: "${name}" (${email}, ${branch}, ${role})`);

      // Supabase에도 저장
      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        SupabaseMode.addEmployee({ name, email, password: '1234', branch, role }).catch(e => console.error('Employee Supabase sync:', e));
      }

      closeModal();
      renderEmployeeManage();
    }

    function closeModal(){document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.remove('show');}

function copyInviteLink() {
  const input = document.getElementById('inviteLinkUrl');
  input.select();
  document.execCommand('copy');
  alert('링크가 복사되었습니다!');
}

function saveInvitation(code) {
  const branch = document.getElementById('inviteBranch').value;
  const maxUses = parseInt(document.getElementById('inviteMax').value);
  const expiryInput = document.getElementById('inviteExpiry').value;
  const expiresAt = expiryInput ? new Date(expiryInput + 'T23:59:59').toISOString() : new Date(Date.now() + 7*24*60*60*1000).toISOString();
  const invites = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_invitations') || '[]');
  invites.push({ code, branch, maxUses, usedCount: 0, expiresAt, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() });
  localStorage.setItem('sop_invitations', JSON.stringify(invites));

  // Supabase에도 저장
  if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
    SupabaseMode.client.from('invitations').insert({
      code, branch, max_uses: maxUses, used_count: 0, expires_at: expiresAt, created_by: user?.id
    }).catch(e => console.error('Invitation save error:', e));
  }

  alert('초대 링크가 활성화되었습니다!\n직원에게 링크를 공유하세요.');
  closeModal();
}

    function exportAllCSV() {
      const emps = getEmployeesWithProgress();
      const h='이름,이메일,지점,진행률,퀴즈평균,상태\n';
      const r = emps.map(e => {
        const st = e.status==='completed'?'완료':e.status==='in_progress'?'진행중':'미시작';
        return `${e.name},${e.email},${e.branch},${e.progress}%,${e.avgScore||0},${st}`;
      }).join('\n');
      const b=new Blob(['\uFEFF'+h+r],{type:'text/csv;charset=utf-8;'});
      const a=document.createElement('a'); a.href=URL.createObjectURL(b); a.download=`sop_report_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`; a.click();
    }

    // PDF 인쇄 전 날짜 세팅
    window.addEventListener('beforeprint', function() {
      const el = document.getElementById('printReportDate');
      if (el) el.textContent = '생성일: ' + new Date().toLocaleDateString('ko-KR', {year:'numeric',month:'long',day:'numeric'});
      if (document.getElementById('page-reports').style.display === 'none') {
        showPage('reports');
      }
    });

    // 리포트 미리보기 (새 창)
    function openReportPreview() {
      const emps = getEmployeesWithProgress();
      const branches = {};
      emps.forEach(e => {
        if (!branches[e.branch]) branches[e.branch] = {total:0,completed:0,avgSum:0};
        branches[e.branch].total++;
        if (e.status==='completed') branches[e.branch].completed++;
        branches[e.branch].avgSum += e.progress;
      });
      const totalEmps = emps.length;
      const completedEmps = emps.filter(e => e.status==='completed').length;
      const completionRate = totalEmps > 0 ? Math.round((completedEmps/totalEmps)*100) : 0;
      const avgScore = totalEmps > 0 ? Math.round(emps.reduce((s,e) => s+(e.avgScore||0), 0)/totalEmps) : 0;
      const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('ko-KR', {year:'numeric',month:'long',day:'numeric'});

      let branchRows = Object.entries(branches).map(([name,d]) => {
        const avg = Math.round(d.avgSum/d.total);
        return `<tr><td>${name}</td><td>${d.total}명</td><td>${d.completed}명</td><td>${avg}%</td></tr>`;
      }).join('');

      const chapters = SopStore.getChapters();
      let chapterRows = chapters.map((ch,i) => {
        const passCount = emps.filter(e => Progress.getEmployeeProgress(e.id).chapterResults[ch.id]?.passed).length;
        const rate = totalEmps > 0 ? Math.round((passCount/totalEmps)*100) : 0;
        return `<tr><td>${i+1}. ${ch.title}</td><td>${passCount}/${totalEmps}명</td><td>${rate}%</td></tr>`;
      }).join('');

      const html = `<!DOCTYPE html><html lang="ko"><head><meta charset="UTF-8">
        <title>SOP 학습 현황 리포트</title>
        <style>
          body{font-family:-apple-system,sans-serif;max-width:800px;margin:0 auto;padding:40px 24px;color:#222;}
          h1{text-align:center;font-size:24px;margin-bottom:4px;}
          .date{text-align:center;color:#888;margin-bottom:32px;font-size:14px;}
          .summary{display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr);gap:16px;margin-bottom:32px;}
          .summary-card{background:#f8f9fa;border-radius:12px;padding:20px;text-align:center;}
          .summary-card .num{font-size:28px;font-weight:700;color:#2563eb;}
          .summary-card .label{font-size:13px;color:#888;margin-top:4px;}
          table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:32px;}
          th{background:#f1f5f9;text-align:left;padding:10px 12px;font-size:13px;font-weight:600;border-bottom:2px solid #e2e8f0;}
          td{padding:10px 12px;font-size:14px;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;}
          h2{font-size:18px;margin:24px 0 12px;padding-bottom:8px;border-bottom:2px solid #2563eb;}
          .footer{text-align:center;color:#aaa;font-size:12px;margin-top:40px;padding-top:16px;border-top:1px solid #eee;}
          .actions{text-align:center;margin-bottom:24px;}
          .actions button{padding:10px 24px;font-size:14px;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;background:#2563eb;color:white;font-weight:600;}
          .actions button:hover{background:#1d4ed8;}
          @media print{.actions{display:none;}}
        </style></head><body>
        <h1>SOP 학습 현황 리포트</h1>
        <p class="date">${today}</p>
        <div class="actions"><button onclick="window.print()">🖨️ 인쇄 / PDF 저장</button></div>
        <div class="summary">
          <div class="summary-card"><div class="num">${totalEmps}</div><div class="label">전체 직원 수</div></div>
          <div class="summary-card"><div class="num">${completionRate}%</div><div class="label">이수율</div></div>
          <div class="summary-card"><div class="num">${avgScore}점</div><div class="label">평균 퀴즈 점수</div></div>
        </div>
        <h2>지점별 학습 현황</h2>
        <table><thead><tr><th>지점</th><th>인원</th><th>이수</th><th>진행률</th></tr></thead><tbody>${branchRows || '<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;color:#aaa;">데이터 없음</td></tr>'}</tbody></table>
        <h2>챕터별 통과율</h2>
        <table><thead><tr><th>챕터</th><th>통과 인원</th><th>통과율</th></tr></thead><tbody>${chapterRows || '<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;color:#aaa;">배포된 SOP가 없습니다</td></tr>'}</tbody></table>
        <div class="footer">Generated by SOP Training System</div>
        </body></html>`;

      const w = window.open('', '_blank');
      w.document.write(html);
      w.document.close();
    }

    // ===== 마감일 관리 =====
    function saveDeadline() {
      const sopId = document.getElementById('deadlineSop').value;
      const branch = document.getElementById('deadlineBranch').value;
      const date = document.getElementById('deadlineDate').value;
      if (!sopId || !date) { alert('SOP와 마감일을 선택하세요'); return; }

      const deadlines = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_deadlines') || '[]');
      const sop = getSops().find(s => s.id === sopId);
      deadlines.push({ id: 'dl-'+Date.now(), sopId, sopTitle: sop?.title || '', branch, deadlineAt: date, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() });
      localStorage.setItem('sop_deadlines', JSON.stringify(deadlines));

      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        SupabaseMode.client.from('deadlines').insert({ sop_id: sopId, branch: branch === 'all' ? '' : branch, deadline_at: date + 'T23:59:59Z' }).catch(e => console.error('Deadline save:', e));
      }

      alert('마감일이 설정되었습니다!');
      renderExistingDeadlines();
    }

    function renderExistingDeadlines() {
      const container = document.getElementById('existingDeadlines');
      if (!container) return;
      const deadlines = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_deadlines') || '[]');
      if (deadlines.length === 0) { container.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--gray-500);">설정된 마감일이 없습니다</p>'; return; }
      container.innerHTML = '<h4 style="font-size:14px;margin-bottom:8px;">설정된 마감일</h4>' + deadlines.map(d => {
        const daysLeft = Math.ceil((new Date(d.deadlineAt) - new Date()) / (1000*60*60*24));
        const color = daysLeft <= 3 ? 'var(--danger)' : daysLeft <= 7 ? 'var(--warning)' : 'var(--gray-700)';
        return `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100);font-size:13px;">
          <span>${d.sopTitle} (${d.branch === 'all' ? '전체' : d.branch})</span>
          <span style="color:${color};font-weight:600;">${d.deadlineAt} (${daysLeft > 0 ? daysLeft + '일 남음' : '만료'})</span>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    function checkDeadlineAlerts() {
      const deadlines = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_deadlines') || '[]');
      const upcoming = deadlines.filter(d => {
        const days = Math.ceil((new Date(d.deadlineAt) - new Date()) / (1000*60*60*24));
        return days > 0 && days <= 7;
      });
      const container = document.getElementById('deadlineAlerts');
      const list = document.getElementById('deadlineList');
      if (!container || !list) return;
      if (upcoming.length === 0) { container.style.display = 'none'; return; }
      container.style.display = 'block';
      list.innerHTML = upcoming.map(d => {
        const days = Math.ceil((new Date(d.deadlineAt) - new Date()) / (1000*60*60*24));
        return `<div style="font-size:13px;padding:4px 0;"><strong>${d.sopTitle}</strong> (${d.branch === 'all' ? '전체' : d.branch}) — <span style="color:var(--danger);font-weight:600;">${days}일 남음</span></div>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    function doLogout() {
      localStorage.removeItem('sop_user');
      window.location.href = '../index.html';
    }

    // ===== AI 영상 생성 =====
    async function generateSopVideos(skipConfirm) {
      if (AI_CONFIG.videoProvider === 'none') {
        alert('영상 생성 기능을 사용하려면 config.js에서 videoProvider를 설정하세요.\n\n추천: SiliconFlow API 키 발급 후\nvideoProvider: "wan" 으로 변경');
        return;
      }
      if (!currentSopId) return;
      const sop = getSops().find(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (!sop || !sop.script) return;

      // Gemini API로 컨텍스트 기반 영어 프롬프트 생성
      async function _buildVideoPrompt(visual, narration) {
        // Gemini로 구체적 프롬프트 생성 시도
        try {
          const geminiPrompt = `You are a video prompt engineer. Convert the following training video scene into a detailed, specific English video generation prompt.

SCENE VISUAL: ${visual || 'N/A'}
SCENE NARRATION: ${narration || 'N/A'}

Requirements:
- Describe a SPECIFIC scene matching the narration content exactly
- Setting: modern Korean kids indoor playground/cafe (키즈카페)
- Characters: staff in uniform performing the described procedures
- Include specific actions, objects, details from the narration
- Style: bright warm lighting, clean professional, training video
- Camera: smooth cinematic movement, 720p quality
- Under 150 words, ONLY the English prompt, nothing else`;

          const result = await AI._callLLM('gemini', geminiPrompt);
          if (result && result.length > 20) {
            console.log('[Video] Gemini prompt:', result.slice(0, 80) + '...');
            return result.trim().replace(/^["']|["']$/g, '');
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.warn('[Video] Gemini prompt failed, using fallback:', e.message);
        }

        // 폴백: 일반적인 교육 장면
        return 'A professional Korean staff member in a bright clean modern workplace. Warm lighting, educational training scene, professional video style, 720p.';
      }

      if (!skipConfirm) {
        const cost = AI_CONFIG.videoProvider === 'wan'
          ? `$${(sop.script.length * 0.29).toFixed(2)}`
          : `$${(sop.script.length * 0.20).toFixed(2)}`;
        if (!confirm(`${sop.script.length}개 씬의 영상을 생성합니다.\n예상 비용: ${cost}\n\n진행하시겠습니까?`)) return;
      }

      // 생성 시작 UI — 페이지 상단 고정 배너
      let statusEl = document.getElementById('videoGenStatus');
      if (statusEl) statusEl.remove();
      const insertTarget = document.getElementById('sopEditorView') || document.getElementById('page-sop');
      insertTarget.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', `
        <div id="videoGenStatus" style="position:sticky; top:0; z-index:100; background:#f5f3ff; border:2px solid #7c3aed; border-radius:12px; padding:16px; margin-bottom:16px;">
          <div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:8px;">
            <h4 style="color:#7c3aed; margin:0;">&#127910; AI 영상 생성 중...</h4>
            <span style="font-size:13px; color:#7c3aed; font-weight:600;" id="videoGenProgress">0/${sop.script.length}</span>
          </div>
          <div id="videoGenLog" style="max-height:250px; overflow-y:auto; font-size:13px;"></div>
        </div>
      `);
      window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

      const log = document.getElementById('videoGenLog');
      const progress = document.getElementById('videoGenProgress');

      for (let i = 0; i < sop.script.length; i++) {
        const scene = sop.script[i];
        const prompt = await _buildVideoPrompt(scene.visual, scene.narration);

        log.innerHTML += `<div style="padding:8px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100); font-size:13px;">
          <strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: 생성 요청 중... <span class="spinner" style="width:14px;height:14px;"></span>
        </div>`;
        progress.textContent = `${i}/${sop.script.length}`;

        let result;
        try {
          result = await AI.generateVideo(prompt, { turbo: false });
          console.log('Video gen result:', JSON.stringify(result));
        } catch(videoErr) {
          console.error('Video gen error:', videoErr);
          result = { status: 'error', message: videoErr.message };
        }

        // 로그 업데이트
        const lastLog = log.lastElementChild;
        if (result.status === 'submitted') {
          lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ⏳ 생성 중... (${result.estimatedCost}) — ID: ${result.requestId?.slice(0,8) || 'N/A'}`;

          // 폴링으로 완료 대기
          const pollResult = await AI.pollVideoUntilDone(result.requestId, (status, attempt) => {
            if (status.status === 'processing') {
              lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ⏳ 생성 중... (${attempt * 10}초 경과)`;
            }
          }, 60); // 최대 10분 대기

          if (pollResult.status === 'completed' && pollResult.videoUrl) {
            const safeNarr = (scene.narration || '').replace(/`/g, "'").replace(/\\/g, '\\\\');
            lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ✅ 완료! <a href="${pollResult.videoUrl}" target="_blank" style="color:var(--primary);">영상 보기</a> <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:2px 10px;font-size:12px;margin-left:6px;" onclick="previewSyncedVideo(\`${pollResult.videoUrl}\`, \`${safeNarr}\`, '씬 ${scene.scene}')">미리보기</button>`;
            // SOP에 영상 URL 저장
            if (!sop.script[i].videoUrl) sop.script[i].videoUrl = pollResult.videoUrl;
          } else if (pollResult.status === 'timeout') {
            lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ⏰ 시간 초과 — 나중에 확인 필요 (ID: ${result.requestId?.slice(0,8)})`;
          } else {
            lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ❌ ${pollResult.message || '생성 실패'}`;
          }
        } else if (result.status === 'error') {
          lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ❌ ${result.message}`;
        } else if (result.status === 'skip') {
          lastLog.innerHTML = `<strong>씬 ${scene.scene}</strong>: ⚠️ ${result.message}`;
          break;
        }
      }

      progress.textContent = `${sop.script.length}/${sop.script.length} 완료`;
      // 영상 URL이 저장된 SOP 업데이트
      const allSops = getSops();
      const sopIdx = allSops.findIndex(s => s.id === currentSopId);
      if (sopIdx !== -1) { allSops[sopIdx] = sop; saveSops(allSops); }

      // TTS 음성 설정 자동 생성
      log.innerHTML += `<div style="padding:8px 0; font-size:13px; color:#7c3aed;">
        &#128266; TTS 음성 생성 중...
      </div>`;
      AI.generateSceneAudio(sop.script, 'ko-KR', currentSopId);
      log.innerHTML += `<div style="padding:12px 0; font-size:14px; font-weight:600; color:#7c3aed;">
        &#127881; 영상 + TTS 음성 생성이 완료되었습니다. 미리보기 버튼으로 확인하세요.
      </div>`;
    }

    // ===== 영상+TTS 동기 미리보기 =====
    let _previewController = null;
    function previewSyncedVideo(videoUrl, narration, sceneLabel) {
      if (_previewController) _previewController.stop();
      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      m.innerHTML = `
        <h3>&#127910; ${sceneLabel} 미리보기</h3>
        <div id="previewVideoContainer" style="background:#000;border-radius:8px 8px 0 0;min-height:200px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;">
          <span class="spinner" style="width:24px;height:24px;border-color:#fff;border-top-color:transparent;"></span>
        </div>
        <div id="previewSubtitleBar" style="background:#000;color:#fff;text-align:center;padding:8px;font-size:14px;border-radius:0 0 8px 8px;min-height:24px;"></div>
        <p style="margin-top:12px;font-size:13px;color:var(--gray-500);line-height:1.6;">${narration}</p>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:16px;">
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="previewSyncedPlay()">&#9654; 재생</button>
          <button class="btn btn-outline" style="flex:1;" onclick="previewSyncedStop();closeModal()">닫기</button>
        </div>
      `;
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');

      _previewController = AI.playSyncedVideo(videoUrl, narration, 'ko-KR');
      const subBar = document.getElementById('previewSubtitleBar');
      _previewController.onSubtitleUpdate = (charIdx, charLen, fullText) => {
        const before = fullText.substring(0, charIdx);
        const word = fullText.substring(charIdx, charIdx + charLen);
        const after = fullText.substring(charIdx + charLen);
        subBar.innerHTML = `${before}<span style="color:#fbbf24;font-weight:bold;">${word}</span>${after.substring(0, 40)}`;
      };
      _previewController.onPlayEnd = () => { subBar.textContent = narration; };
      _previewController.play(document.getElementById('previewVideoContainer'));
    }
    function previewSyncedPlay() {
      if (_previewController) _previewController.resume();
    }
    function previewSyncedStop() {
      if (_previewController) { _previewController.stop(); _previewController = null; }
    }

    // ===== AI 설정 페이지 =====
    function renderSettings() {
      // 현재 값을 셀렉트에 반영
      document.getElementById('setScript').value = AI_CONFIG.scriptProvider;
      document.getElementById('setQuiz').value = AI_CONFIG.quizProvider;
      document.getElementById('setChat').value = AI_CONFIG.chatProvider;
      document.getElementById('setVideo').value = AI_CONFIG.videoProvider;

      // 저장된 키 반영 (마스킹)
      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_ai_keys') || '{}');
      ['gemini','groq','openai','siliconflow'].forEach(k => {
        const input = document.getElementById('key' + k.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + k.slice(1));
        if (input && saved[k]) input.value = saved[k];
      });

      updateAiStatusDisplay();
    }

    function updateAiConfig() {
      AI_CONFIG.scriptProvider = document.getElementById('setScript').value;
      AI_CONFIG.quizProvider = document.getElementById('setQuiz').value;
      AI_CONFIG.chatProvider = document.getElementById('setChat').value;
      AI_CONFIG.videoProvider = document.getElementById('setVideo').value;

      // localStorage에 설정 저장
      localStorage.setItem('sop_ai_config', JSON.stringify({
        scriptProvider: AI_CONFIG.scriptProvider,
        quizProvider: AI_CONFIG.quizProvider,
        chatProvider: AI_CONFIG.chatProvider,
        videoProvider: AI_CONFIG.videoProvider,
      }));

      AuditLog.add('system', 'ai_config', `AI 설정 변경 — 스크립트:${AI_CONFIG.scriptProvider}, 퀴즈:${AI_CONFIG.quizProvider}, 챗봇:${AI_CONFIG.chatProvider}`);
      updateAiStatusDisplay();
    }

    function updateAiKeys() {
      const keys = {
        gemini: document.getElementById('keyGemini').value.trim(),
        groq: document.getElementById('keyGroq').value.trim(),
        openai: document.getElementById('keyOpenai').value.trim(),
        siliconflow: document.getElementById('keySiliconflow').value.trim(),
      };

      // AI_CONFIG에 반영
      Object.assign(AI_CONFIG.keys, keys);

      // localStorage에 저장
      localStorage.setItem('sop_ai_keys', JSON.stringify(keys));

      updateAiStatusDisplay();
    }

    function updateAiStatusDisplay() {
      const status = AI.getStatus();
      const display = document.getElementById('aiStatusDisplay');
      if (!display) return;

      display.innerHTML = Object.entries(status).filter(([k]) => k !== 'monthlyCost').map(([k, v]) => {
        const labels = { script: '스크립트', quiz: '퀴즈', chat: '챗봇', tts: 'TTS', video: '영상' };
        const isActive = !v.includes('미사용') && !v.includes('none');
        const color = v.includes('무료') ? 'var(--success)' : v.includes('미사용') ? 'var(--gray-500)' : 'var(--primary)';
        return `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100);">
          <span style="font-size:14px;">${labels[k] || k}</span>
          <span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:${color};">${v}</span>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');

      const costEl = document.getElementById('aiCostDisplay');
      if (costEl) costEl.textContent = `예상 월 비용: ${status.monthlyCost}`;
    }

    // 저장된 AI 설정 복원
    (function restoreAiConfig() {
      const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_ai_config') || 'null');
      if (saved) {
        Object.assign(AI_CONFIG, saved);
      }
      const keys = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_ai_keys') || 'null');
      if (keys) {
        Object.assign(AI_CONFIG.keys, keys);
      }
    })();

    // ===== SOP 버전 이력 =====
    function getVersions(sopId) {
      return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_versions_' + sopId) || '[]');
    }

    function saveVersionSnapshot(sopId, data) {
      const versions = getVersions(sopId);
      const lastVersion = versions.length > 0 ? versions[versions.length - 1].version : 0;
      const snapshot = {
        version: lastVersion + 1,
        title: data.title,
        content: data.content,
        savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        savedBy: user?.name || user?.email || 'admin'
      };
      versions.push(snapshot);
      localStorage.setItem('sop_versions_' + sopId, JSON.stringify(versions));

      // Supabase sync if available
      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        SupabaseMode.client.from('sops').update({
          version: snapshot.version,
          updated_at: snapshot.savedAt
        }).eq('id', sopId).catch(e => console.error('Version Supabase sync:', e));
      }
    }

    function showVersionHistory() {
      if (!currentSopId) return;
      const versions = getVersions(currentSopId);
      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');

      if (versions.length === 0) {
        m.innerHTML = `<h3>&#128203; 버전 이력</h3>
          <p style="color:var(--gray-500); text-align:center; padding:40px 0;">저장된 버전이 없습니다.<br>SOP를 저장하면 자동으로 버전이 기록됩니다.</p>
          <button class="btn btn-outline" style="width:100%; margin-top:16px;" onclick="closeModal()">닫기</button>`;
        document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
        return;
      }

      const listHTML = versions.slice().reverse().map(v => {
        const d = new Date(v.savedAt);
        const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString('ko-KR') + ' ' + d.toLocaleTimeString('ko-KR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        return `<div style="display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; padding:12px 0; border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100);">
          <div>
            <strong style="font-size:14px;">v${v.version}</strong>
            <span style="font-size:13px; color:var(--gray-500); margin-left:8px;">${v.title}</span>
            <div style="font-size:12px; color:var(--gray-400);">${dateStr} &middot; ${v.savedBy}</div>
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex; gap:6px;">
            <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:4px 10px; font-size:12px;" onclick="previewVersion('${currentSopId}', ${v.version})">미리보기</button>
            <button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:4px 10px; font-size:12px; color:var(--primary); border-color:var(--primary);" onclick="restoreVersion('${currentSopId}', ${v.version})">복원</button>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');

      m.innerHTML = `<h3>&#128203; 버전 이력 (${versions.length}개)</h3>
        <div style="max-height:400px; overflow-y:auto;">${listHTML}</div>
        <button class="btn btn-outline" style="width:100%; margin-top:16px;" onclick="closeModal()">닫기</button>`;
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
    }

    function previewVersion(sopId, versionNum) {
      const versions = getVersions(sopId);
      const v = versions.find(ver => ver.version === versionNum);
      if (!v) return;

      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      const d = new Date(v.savedAt);
      const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString('ko-KR') + ' ' + d.toLocaleTimeString('ko-KR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });

      m.innerHTML = `<div style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; margin-bottom:16px;">
          <h3 style="margin:0;">v${v.version} — ${v.title}</h3>
          <span style="font-size:12px; color:var(--gray-500);">${dateStr}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="border:1px solid var(--gray-200); border-radius:var(--radius); padding:20px; background:var(--gray-50); max-height:400px; overflow-y:auto; font-size:14px; line-height:1.7;">
          ${v.content}
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex; gap:8px; margin-top:16px;">
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="restoreVersion('${sopId}', ${versionNum})">이 버전으로 복원</button>
          <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="showVersionHistory()">목록으로</button>
        </div>`;
    }

    function restoreVersion(sopId, versionNum) {
      const versions = getVersions(sopId);
      const v = versions.find(ver => ver.version === versionNum);
      if (!v) return;
      if (!confirm(`v${v.version} 버전으로 복원하시겠습니까?\n현재 내용은 자동으로 새 버전으로 저장됩니다.`)) return;

      // Save current state as a new version before restoring
      const currentTitle = document.getElementById('sopTitleInput').value || '제목 없음';
      const currentContent = document.getElementById('sopEditor').innerHTML;
      saveVersionSnapshot(sopId, { title: currentTitle, content: currentContent, category: document.getElementById('sopCategory').value });

      // Restore
      document.getElementById('sopTitleInput').value = v.title;
      document.getElementById('sopEditor').innerHTML = v.content;
      saveSop();
      closeModal();
    }

    // ===== 학습 경로 관리 =====
    function getLearningPaths() {
      return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_learning_paths') || '{}');
    }

    function saveLearningPaths(paths) {
      localStorage.setItem('sop_learning_paths', JSON.stringify(paths));
      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        SupabaseMode.client.from('settings').upsert({
          key: 'learning_paths', value: JSON.stringify(paths), updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
        }, { onConflict: 'key' }).catch(e => console.error('Learning path Supabase sync:', e));
      }
    }

    function getBranchNames() {
      const emps = EmployeeStore.getAll();
      const branches = [...new Set(emps.map(e => e.branch).filter(Boolean))].sort();
      // Include known branches even if no employees yet
      const known = ['서울 강남점','서울 홍대점','부산 해운대점','호치민 1호점','하노이 1호점'];
      known.forEach(b => { if (!branches.includes(b)) branches.push(b); });
      return branches.sort();
    }

    function renderLearningPaths() {
      const paths = getLearningPaths();
      const branches = getBranchNames();
      const sops = getSops().filter(s => s.status === 'published');
      const tbody = document.getElementById('lpTableBody');

      if (sops.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center; padding:40px; color:var(--gray-500);">배포된 SOP가 없습니다. SOP를 먼저 배포하세요.</td></tr>`;
        return;
      }

      tbody.innerHTML = branches.map(branch => {
        const assigned = paths[branch]; // undefined means all
        const allAssigned = !assigned || assigned.length === sops.length;
        const assignedSops = allAssigned
          ? sops
          : sops.filter(s => assigned.includes(s.id));
        const sopNames = allAssigned
          ? `<span class="badge" style="background:#dcfce7; color:var(--success);">전체 배정 (${sops.length}개)</span>`
          : assignedSops.length > 0
            ? assignedSops.map(s => `<span class="badge" style="background:var(--primary-light); color:var(--primary);">${s.title}</span>`).join(' ')
            : `<span class="badge" style="background:var(--gray-100); color:var(--danger);">미배정</span>`;

        return `<tr>
          <td><strong>${branch}</strong></td>
          <td style="max-width:400px;">${sopNames}</td>
          <td><button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:6px 14px; font-size:13px;" onclick="editLearningPath('${branch.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">편집</button></td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    function editLearningPath(branch) {
      const paths = getLearningPaths();
      const sops = getSops().filter(s => s.status === 'published');
      const assigned = paths[branch]; // undefined = all
      const allAssigned = !assigned;

      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');
      m.innerHTML = `
        <h3>학습 경로 편집 — ${branch}</h3>
        <p style="font-size:14px; color:var(--gray-500); margin-bottom:16px;">이 지점 직원에게 배정할 SOP를 선택하세요</p>
        <div style="margin-bottom:16px;">
          <label style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:8px; padding:10px; background:var(--gray-50); border-radius:8px; cursor:pointer; font-weight:600;">
            <input type="checkbox" id="lpAssignAll" onchange="toggleAssignAll()" ${allAssigned ? 'checked' : ''}> 전체 배정 (모든 SOP)
          </label>
        </div>
        <div id="lpSopChecklist" style="${allAssigned ? 'opacity:0.5; pointer-events:none;' : ''}">
          ${sops.map(s => {
            const checked = allAssigned || (assigned && assigned.includes(s.id));
            return `<label style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:10px; padding:10px 12px; border-bottom:1px solid var(--gray-100); cursor:pointer;">
              <input type="checkbox" class="lp-sop-cb" value="${s.id}" ${checked ? 'checked' : ''}>
              <div>
                <strong style="font-size:14px;">${s.title}</strong>
                <div style="font-size:12px; color:var(--gray-500);">${s.category} · ${s.script ? s.script.length + '씬' : '스크립트 없음'}</div>
              </div>
            </label>`;
          }).join('')}
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex; gap:8px; margin-top:20px;">
          <button class="btn btn-primary" style="flex:1;" onclick="saveLearningPath('${branch.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">저장</button>
          <button class="btn btn-outline" onclick="closeModal()">취소</button>
        </div>`;
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
    }

    function toggleAssignAll() {
      const checked = document.getElementById('lpAssignAll').checked;
      const list = document.getElementById('lpSopChecklist');
      list.style.opacity = checked ? '0.5' : '1';
      list.style.pointerEvents = checked ? 'none' : 'auto';
      if (checked) {
        list.querySelectorAll('.lp-sop-cb').forEach(cb => cb.checked = true);
      }
    }

    function saveLearningPath(branch) {
      const paths = getLearningPaths();
      const allChecked = document.getElementById('lpAssignAll').checked;

      if (allChecked) {
        delete paths[branch]; // undefined = all SOPs
      } else {
        const checked = [...document.querySelectorAll('.lp-sop-cb:checked')].map(cb => cb.value);
        paths[branch] = checked;
      }

      saveLearningPaths(paths);
      closeModal();
      renderLearningPaths();
    }

    // ===== MBTI 관련 함수 =====
    function getEmployeeMbti(email) {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('sop_mbti_' + email);
      if (!raw) return null;
      try { return JSON.parse(raw); } catch(e) { return null; }
    }

    // ===== 등급 관련 함수 =====
    function getEmployeeGrade(email) {
      const chapters = SopStore.getChapters();
      const scores = [];
      chapters.forEach(ch => {
        // Try user-scoped key format first
        const userRaw = localStorage.getItem('sop_exam_results_' + email + '_' + ch.id);
        if (userRaw) {
          try {
            const data = JSON.parse(userRaw);
            const s = data.score != null ? data.score : (typeof data === 'number' ? data : null);
            if (s != null) scores.push(s);
          } catch(e) {}
          return;
        }
        // Fallback: legacy key format
        const raw = localStorage.getItem('sop_exam_results_' + ch.id);
        if (!raw) return;
        try {
          const results = JSON.parse(raw);
          if (Array.isArray(results)) {
            const match = results.find(r => r.email === email);
            if (match && match.score != null) scores.push(match.score);
          } else if (results[email] != null) {
            scores.push(typeof results[email] === 'object' ? results[email].score : results[email]);
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      });
      // Also try progress-based scores
      if (scores.length === 0) {
        const emp = EmployeeStore.getAll().find(e => e.email === email);
        if (emp) {
          const prog = Progress.getEmployeeProgress(emp.id);
          Object.values(prog.chapterResults).forEach(r => {
            if (r.score > 0) scores.push(r.score);
          });
        }
      }
      if (scores.length === 0) return null;
      const avg = Math.round(scores.reduce((a,b) => a + b, 0) / scores.length);
      return scoreToGrade(avg);
    }

    function scoreToGrade(avg) {
      if (avg >= 95) return { grade: 'S', color: '#92400e', bg: '#fef3c7' };
      if (avg >= 85) return { grade: 'A', color: '#166534', bg: '#dcfce7' };
      if (avg >= 75) return { grade: 'B', color: '#1e40af', bg: '#dbeafe' };
      if (avg >= 65) return { grade: 'C', color: '#854d0e', bg: '#fef9c3' };
      if (avg >= 50) return { grade: 'D', color: '#9a3412', bg: '#ffedd5' };
      return { grade: 'F', color: '#991b1b', bg: '#fee2e2' };
    }

    // ===== MBTI 상세 모달 =====
    function showMbtiDetail(name, email) {
      const data = getEmployeeMbti(email);
      if (!data) return;
      const m = document.getElementById('modalContent');

      // Dimension bars
      const dims = [
        { left: 'E', right: 'I', leftLabel: '외향(E)', rightLabel: '내향(I)', score: data.dimensions?.E ?? data.dimensions?.EI ?? 50 },
        { left: 'S', right: 'N', leftLabel: '감각(S)', rightLabel: '직관(N)', score: data.dimensions?.S ?? data.dimensions?.SN ?? 50 },
        { left: 'T', right: 'F', leftLabel: '사고(T)', rightLabel: '감정(F)', score: data.dimensions?.T ?? data.dimensions?.TF ?? 50 },
        { left: 'J', right: 'P', leftLabel: '판단(J)', rightLabel: '인식(P)', score: data.dimensions?.J ?? data.dimensions?.JP ?? 50 },
      ];

      const barsHtml = dims.map(d => {
        const leftPct = d.score;
        const rightPct = 100 - d.score;
        return `<div style="margin-bottom:12px;">
          <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:4px;">
            <span style="font-weight:600;">${d.leftLabel} ${leftPct}%</span>
            <span style="font-weight:600;">${d.rightLabel} ${rightPct}%</span>
          </div>
          <div style="display:flex;height:8px;border-radius:4px;overflow:hidden;background:var(--gray-200);">
            <div style="width:${leftPct}%;background:#7c3aed;border-radius:4px 0 0 4px;"></div>
            <div style="width:${rightPct}%;background:#c4b5fd;border-radius:0 4px 4px 0;"></div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');

      const testDate = data.testDate ? new Date(data.testDate).toLocaleDateString('ko-KR') : '-';

      m.innerHTML = `
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:16px;margin-bottom:20px;">
          <div style="width:64px;height:64px;border-radius:16px;background:#ede9fe;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;">
            <span style="font-size:24px;font-weight:800;color:#7c3aed;">${data.type || '?'}</span>
          </div>
          <div>
            <h3 style="margin-bottom:2px;">${name}</h3>
            <p style="font-size:14px;color:var(--gray-500);">MBTI: <strong style="color:#7c3aed;">${data.type || '-'}</strong></p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <h4 style="font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px;">차원별 점수</h4>
        ${barsHtml}
        ${data.description ? `<div style="margin-top:16px;padding:16px;background:var(--gray-50);border-radius:8px;">
          <h4 style="font-size:14px;margin-bottom:8px;">성격 설명</h4>
          <p style="font-size:13px;line-height:1.6;color:var(--gray-700);">${data.description}</p>
        </div>` : ''}
        ${data.workStyle ? `<div style="margin-top:12px;padding:16px;background:#ede9fe;border-radius:8px;">
          <h4 style="font-size:14px;margin-bottom:8px;color:#7c3aed;">업무 스타일 팁</h4>
          <p style="font-size:13px;line-height:1.6;color:#5b21b6;">${data.workStyle}</p>
        </div>` : ''}
        <p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);margin-top:12px;">검사일: ${testDate}</p>
        <button class="btn btn-outline" style="width:100%;margin-top:16px;" onclick="closeModal()">닫기</button>
      `;
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('show');
    }

    // ===== AI 대화 로그 =====
    function renderChatLogs() {
      const allLogs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_chat_logs') || '[]');
      const logs = getFilteredChatLogs(allLogs);
      const searchQ = (document.getElementById('chatLogSearch')?.value || '').toLowerCase();

      // Filter by search
      const filtered = searchQ
        ? logs.filter(l => (l.employeeName || l.userName || '').toLowerCase().includes(searchQ))
        : logs;

      // Stats
      const totalQ = filtered.length;
      const userSet = new Set(filtered.map(l => l.employeeName || l.userName || l.email || 'Unknown'));
      document.getElementById('chatLogTotalQ').textContent = totalQ;
      document.getElementById('chatLogActiveUsers').textContent = userSet.size;

      // Per-employee question count
      const perEmp = {};
      filtered.forEach(l => {
        const name = l.employeeName || l.userName || l.email || 'Unknown';
        perEmp[name] = (perEmp[name] || 0) + 1;
      });
      document.getElementById('chatLogPerEmployee').innerHTML = Object.entries(perEmp)
        .sort((a,b) => b[1] - a[1])
        .map(([name, count]) => `<span class="badge" style="background:var(--primary-light);color:var(--primary);">${name}: ${count}건</span>`)
        .join('');

      // Table (most recent first, limit 100)
      const rows = filtered.slice().reverse().slice(0, 100);
      document.getElementById('chatLogBody').innerHTML = rows.length > 0
        ? rows.map(l => {
            const ts = l.timestamp ? new Date(l.timestamp).toLocaleString('ko-KR', { month:'short', day:'numeric', hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit' }) : '-';
            const name = l.employeeName || l.userName || l.email || '-';
            const q = (l.question || l.message || '').length > 80 ? (l.question || l.message || '').slice(0,80) + '...' : (l.question || l.message || '-');
            const a = (l.answer || l.response || '').length > 80 ? (l.answer || l.response || '').slice(0,80) + '...' : (l.answer || l.response || '-');
            return `<tr><td style="font-size:12px;color:var(--gray-500);white-space:nowrap;">${ts}</td>
              <td style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;">${name}</td>
              <td style="font-size:13px;max-width:250px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${q}</td>
              <td style="font-size:13px;max-width:250px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;color:var(--gray-600);">${a}</td></tr>`;
          }).join('')
        : `<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--gray-500);">대화 기록이 없습니다.<br>직원이 AI 챗봇을 사용하면 여기에 기록됩니다.</td></tr>`;
    }

    // ===== 대시보드 통계 업데이트 (평균 등급 + MBTI 응시율) =====
    function updateDashboardExtraStats() {
      const emps = EmployeeStore.getAll();
      if (emps.length === 0) return;

      // MBTI 응시율
      let mbtiCount = 0;
      emps.forEach(emp => {
        if (getEmployeeMbti(emp.email)) mbtiCount++;
      });
      const mbtiRate = Math.round((mbtiCount / emps.length) * 100);
      const mbtiEl = document.getElementById('statMbtiRate');
      if (mbtiEl) mbtiEl.textContent = mbtiRate + '%';

      // 평균 등급
      const gradeValues = { S: 5, A: 4, B: 3, C: 2, D: 1, F: 0 };
      let gradeSum = 0, gradeCount = 0;
      emps.forEach(emp => {
        const g = getEmployeeGrade(emp.email);
        if (g) { gradeSum += gradeValues[g.grade] || 0; gradeCount++; }
      });
      const avgEl = document.getElementById('statAvgGrade');
      if (avgEl) {
        if (gradeCount === 0) { avgEl.textContent = '-'; return; }
        const avgVal = gradeSum / gradeCount;
        let avgGrade = 'F';
        if (avgVal >= 4.5) avgGrade = 'S';
        else if (avgVal >= 3.5) avgGrade = 'A';
        else if (avgVal >= 2.5) avgGrade = 'B';
        else if (avgVal >= 1.5) avgGrade = 'C';
        else if (avgVal >= 0.5) avgGrade = 'D';
        const gi = scoreToGrade(avgGrade === 'S' ? 95 : avgGrade === 'A' ? 85 : avgGrade === 'B' ? 75 : avgGrade === 'C' ? 65 : avgGrade === 'D' ? 50 : 30);
        avgEl.textContent = avgGrade;
        avgEl.style.color = gi.color;
      }
    }

    // Patch renderDashboard to include extra stats
    const _origRenderDashboard = renderDashboard;
    renderDashboard = function() {
      _origRenderDashboard();
      updateDashboardExtraStats();
    };

    // ===== 알림 보내기 =====
    function sendNotification() {
      const target = document.getElementById('notifTarget').value;
      const type = document.getElementById('notifType').value;
      const message = document.getElementById('notifMessage').value.trim();
      if (!message) { alert('메시지를 입력하세요'); return; }

      const typeLabels = { reminder: '학습 리마인더', deadline: '마감일 알림', newSop: '새 SOP 알림', custom: '관리자 메시지' };
      const targetLabels = { all: '전체', incomplete: '미학습자', specific: '특정 직원' };

      let targetEmails = null;
      if (target === 'specific') {
        const sel = document.getElementById('notifSpecificEmps');
        targetEmails = [...sel.selectedOptions].map(o => o.value);
        if (targetEmails.length === 0) { alert('직원을 선택하세요'); return; }
      }

      const notif = {
        id: 'notif-' + Date.now(),
        target,
        targetEmails,
        type,
        title: 'SOP Training',
        message,
        sentAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        sentBy: user?.name || user?.email || 'admin',
        targetLabel: targetLabels[target] || target,
        typeLabel: typeLabels[type] || type
      };
