      // 대기 중 알림에 추가 (직원 앱에서 읽음)
      const pending = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_pending_notifications') || '[]');
      pending.push(notif);
      localStorage.setItem('sop_pending_notifications', JSON.stringify(pending));

      // 이력에 추가
      const history = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_notification_history') || '[]');
      history.push(notif);
      localStorage.setItem('sop_notification_history', JSON.stringify(history));

      closeModal();
      renderNotifHistory();
      alert('알림이 발송되었습니다!\n직원이 앱을 열면 알림이 표시됩니다.');
    }

    function renderNotifHistory() {
      const history = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_notification_history') || '[]');
      const tbody = document.getElementById('notifHistoryBody');
      if (!tbody) return;

      if (history.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center; padding:40px; color:var(--gray-500);">발송된 알림이 없습니다</td></tr>';
        return;
      }

      tbody.innerHTML = history.slice().reverse().map(n => {
        const date = new Date(n.sentAt).toLocaleString('ko-KR', { month:'short', day:'numeric', hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit' });
        const targetText = n.targetLabel + (n.targetEmails ? ' (' + n.targetEmails.length + '명)' : '');
        const typeBadge = n.type === 'reminder' ? 'background:var(--primary-light);color:var(--primary);'
          : n.type === 'deadline' ? 'background:#fef3c7;color:#92400e;'
          : n.type === 'newSop' ? 'background:#dcfce7;color:var(--success);'
          : 'background:var(--gray-100);color:var(--gray-700);';
        return `<tr>
          <td style="font-size:13px;white-space:nowrap;">${date}</td>
          <td style="font-size:13px;">${targetText}</td>
          <td style="font-size:13px;max-width:300px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${n.message}</td>
          <td><span class="badge" style="${typeBadge}">${n.typeLabel}</span></td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    // ===== 감사 로그 유틸리티 =====
    const AuditLog = {
      KEY: 'sop_audit_log',
      MAX_ENTRIES: 500,

      _getAdmin() {
        const user = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_user') || 'null');
        return user ? user.name || user.email || 'Unknown' : 'System';
      },

      add(type, action, detail = '') {
        const logs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.KEY) || '[]');
        logs.unshift({
          id: Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6),
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          admin: this._getAdmin(),
          type,    // sop, employee, publish, auth, system
          action,  // create, edit, delete, publish, unpublish, login, etc.
          detail
        });
        // 최대 개수 제한
        if (logs.length > this.MAX_ENTRIES) logs.length = this.MAX_ENTRIES;
        localStorage.setItem(this.KEY, JSON.stringify(logs));
      },

      getAll() {
        return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this.KEY) || '[]');
      },

      getFiltered(type) {
        const all = this.getAll();
        if (!type || type === 'all') return all;
        return all.filter(l => l.type === type);
      },

      clear() {
        localStorage.removeItem(this.KEY);
      },

      exportCSV() {
        const logs = this.getAll();
        if (logs.length === 0) { alert('내보낼 로그가 없습니다.'); return; }
        const header = '시간,관리자,유형,활동내용\n';
        const rows = logs.map(l => {
          const time = new Date(l.timestamp).toLocaleString('ko-KR');
          const detail = (l.detail || '').replace(/"/g, '""');
          return `"${time}","${l.admin}","${l.type}","${detail}"`;
        }).join('\n');
        const blob = new Blob(['\uFEFF' + header + rows], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = url;
        a.download = `audit_log_${new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10)}.csv`;
        a.click();
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
      }
    };

    let auditLogPage = 1;
    const AUDIT_PAGE_SIZE = 30;

    function renderAuditLog() {
      const filter = document.getElementById('auditFilterType')?.value || 'all';
      const logs = AuditLog.getFiltered(filter);
      const tbody = document.getElementById('auditLogBody');
      if (!tbody) return;

      if (logs.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--gray-400);">감사 로그가 없습니다</td></tr>`;
        document.getElementById('auditLogPagination').innerHTML = '';
        return;
      }

      const totalPages = Math.ceil(logs.length / AUDIT_PAGE_SIZE);
      if (auditLogPage > totalPages) auditLogPage = totalPages;
      const start = (auditLogPage - 1) * AUDIT_PAGE_SIZE;
      const pageItems = logs.slice(start, start + AUDIT_PAGE_SIZE);

      const typeColors = {
        sop: 'background:#EFF6FF;color:#2563EB;',
        employee: 'background:#F0FDF4;color:#16A34A;',
        publish: 'background:#FDF4FF;color:#9333EA;',
        auth: 'background:#FEF3C7;color:#D97706;',
        system: 'background:#F1F5F9;color:#475569;'
      };
      const typeLabels = { sop: 'SOP', employee: '직원', publish: '배포', auth: '인증', system: '시스템' };

      tbody.innerHTML = pageItems.map(l => {
        const time = new Date(l.timestamp).toLocaleString('ko-KR', { month:'2-digit', day:'2-digit', hour:'2-digit', minute:'2-digit', second:'2-digit' });
        const badge = typeColors[l.type] || typeColors.system;
        const label = typeLabels[l.type] || l.type;
        return `<tr>
          <td style="white-space:nowrap;color:var(--gray-500);">${time}</td>
          <td style="font-weight:500;">${l.admin}</td>
          <td><span class="badge" style="${badge};padding:3px 8px;border-radius:4px;font-size:11px;">${label}</span></td>
          <td style="max-width:400px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">${l.detail || l.action}</td>
        </tr>`;
      }).join('');

      // 페이지네이션
      const pagDiv = document.getElementById('auditLogPagination');
      if (totalPages <= 1) { pagDiv.innerHTML = `<span style="color:var(--gray-400);font-size:12px;">총 ${logs.length}건</span>`; return; }
      let pagHtml = `<span style="color:var(--gray-400);font-size:12px;margin-right:12px;">총 ${logs.length}건</span>`;
      if (auditLogPage > 1) pagHtml += `<button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:4px 12px;font-size:12px;margin:0 2px;" onclick="auditLogPage--;renderAuditLog();">이전</button>`;
      pagHtml += `<span style="font-size:13px;margin:0 8px;">${auditLogPage} / ${totalPages}</span>`;
      if (auditLogPage < totalPages) pagHtml += `<button class="btn btn-outline" style="padding:4px 12px;font-size:12px;margin:0 2px;" onclick="auditLogPage++;renderAuditLog();">다음</button>`;
      pagDiv.innerHTML = pagHtml;
    }

    function exportAuditLog() { AuditLog.exportCSV(); }
    function clearAuditLog() {
      if (!confirm('모든 감사 로그를 삭제하시겠습니까?')) return;
      AuditLog.clear();
      renderAuditLog();
    }

    // ===== 초기화 =====
    // 관리자 접속 기록
    AuditLog.add('auth', 'admin_access', `관리자 페이지 접속: ${AuditLog._getAdmin()}`);
    renderSopList();
    applySopPagePermissions();
  </script>

</body>
</html>

    document.getElementById('alreadyHaveAccount').textContent = t.alreadyHaveAccount;

    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const inviteCode = urlParams.get('code');
    let currentInvite = null;

    async function init() {
      if (!inviteCode) {
        showInvalid();
        return;
      }

      // Supabase 초기화
      await SupabaseMode.init();

      // 초대 코드 검증
      let invite = null;

      // 1) Supabase에서 확인
      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        try {
          const { data } = await SupabaseMode.client
            .from('invitations')
            .select('*')
            .eq('code', inviteCode)
            .single();
          if (data && data.used_count < data.max_uses) {
            if (data.expires_at && new Date(data.expires_at) < new Date()) {
              showExpired();
              return;
            }
            invite = {
              code: data.code,
              branch: data.branch,
              maxUses: data.max_uses,
              usedCount: data.used_count,
              expiresAt: data.expires_at
            };
          }
        } catch(e) { console.log('Supabase invite check:', e); }
      }

      // 2) localStorage에서 확인 (폴백)
      if (!invite) {
        const invites = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_invitations') || '[]');
        const local = invites.find(i => i.code === inviteCode && i.usedCount < i.maxUses);
        if (local) {
          if (local.expiresAt && new Date(local.expiresAt) < new Date()) {
            showExpired();
            return;
          }
          invite = local;
        }
      }

      if (!invite) {
        showInvalid();
        return;
      }

      currentInvite = invite;
      document.getElementById('inviteInfo').textContent = t.staffRegistration(invite.branch);
      document.getElementById('regBranch').value = invite.branch;
      document.getElementById('registerForm').style.display = 'block';
    }

    function showInvalid() {
      document.getElementById('inviteInfo').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('invalidMsg').style.display = 'block';
    }

    function showExpired() {
      document.getElementById('inviteInfo').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('errorMsg').textContent = t.expired;
      document.getElementById('errorMsg').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('invalidMsg').style.display = 'block';
      document.getElementById('invalidTitle').textContent = t.expired;
    }

    document.getElementById('registerForm').addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      const name = document.getElementById('regName').value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('regEmail').value.trim();
      const password = document.getElementById('regPassword').value;

      if (!name || !email || password.length < 4) {
        document.getElementById('errorMsg').textContent = t.fillAllFields;
        document.getElementById('errorMsg').style.display = 'block';
        return;
      }

      // 이메일 중복 체크
      const existing = EmployeeStore.getAll();
      if (existing.find(e => e.email === email)) {
        document.getElementById('errorMsg').textContent = t.emailExists;
        document.getElementById('errorMsg').style.display = 'block';
        return;
      }

      // 직원 등록
      const newEmp = {
        id: 'emp-' + Date.now(),
        name, email, branch: currentInvite.branch,
        role: 'staff',
        created: new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10)
      };

      existing.push(newEmp);
      EmployeeStore.save(existing);

      // Supabase에도 저장 (비밀번호 해시 처리)
      if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
        try {
          let pwHash = password;
          try {
            const hashRes = await fetch('/api/auth', {
              method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
              body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'hash', password })
            });
            const hashData = await hashRes.json();
            if (hashData.hash) pwHash = hashData.hash;
          } catch(e) { console.warn('Hash failed, using plain:', e); }

          await SupabaseMode.client.from('employees').insert({
            name, email, password_hash: pwHash,
            branch: currentInvite.branch, role: 'staff'
          });

          // 초대 사용 횟수 증가
          await SupabaseMode.client.from('invitations')
            .update({ used_count: currentInvite.usedCount + 1 })
            .eq('code', currentInvite.code);
        } catch(e) { console.error('Supabase register error:', e); }
      }

      // localStorage 초대 사용 횟수 업데이트
      const invites = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sop_invitations') || '[]');
      const idx = invites.findIndex(i => i.code === currentInvite.code);
      if (idx !== -1) {
        invites[idx].usedCount++;
        localStorage.setItem('sop_invitations', JSON.stringify(invites));
      }

      // 성공 표시
      document.getElementById('registerForm').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('inviteInfo').style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('successMsg').style.display = 'block';
    });

    init();
  </script>
</body>
</html>

    let currentLang = localStorage.getItem('sop_lang') || CONFIG.DEFAULT_LANG;

    function T(key) {
      return (TEXTS[currentLang] || TEXTS.ko)[key] || key;
    }

    function setLang(lang) {
      currentLang = lang;
      localStorage.setItem('sop_lang', lang);
      updateTexts();
    }

    function updateTexts() {
      document.getElementById('pageTitle').textContent = T('pageTitle');
      document.getElementById('pageDesc').textContent = T('pageDesc');
      document.getElementById('labelCurrent').textContent = T('labelCurrent');
      document.getElementById('labelNew').textContent = T('labelNew');
      document.getElementById('labelConfirm').textContent = T('labelConfirm');
      document.getElementById('submitBtn').textContent = T('submit');
      document.getElementById('backLink').textContent = T('backLink');
      // Nav labels
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-i18n]').forEach(el => {
        const key = el.getAttribute('data-i18n');
        if (T(key) !== key) el.textContent = T(key);
      });
    }

    updateTexts();

    // ===== Toggle password visibility =====
    function togglePw(inputId, btn) {
      const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
      if (input.type === 'password') {
        input.type = 'text';
        btn.innerHTML = '&#128064;';
      } else {
        input.type = 'password';
        btn.innerHTML = '&#128065;';
      }
    }

    // ===== Password strength meter =====
    const newPwInput = document.getElementById('newPw');
    newPwInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
      const val = newPwInput.value;
      const bars = document.querySelectorAll('.pw-strength-bar');
      const textEl = document.getElementById('strengthText');
      let score = 0;

      if (val.length >= 4) score++;
      if (val.length >= 8) score++;
      if (/[A-Z]/.test(val) && /[a-z]/.test(val)) score++;
      if (/[0-9]/.test(val) && /[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(val)) score++;

      const colors = ['#ef4444', '#f59e0b', '#22c55e', '#16a34a'];
      const labels = ['strengthWeak', 'strengthFair', 'strengthGood', 'strengthStrong'];

      bars.forEach((bar, i) => {
        bar.style.background = i < score ? colors[Math.min(score - 1, 3)] : 'var(--gray-100)';
      });

      if (val.length > 0) {
        textEl.textContent = T(labels[Math.min(score - 1, 3)] || labels[0]);
        textEl.style.color = colors[Math.min(score - 1, 3)];
      } else {
        textEl.textContent = '';
      }

      // Clear error on typing
      clearFieldError('newPw', 'errorNew');
    });

    // ===== Field error helpers =====
    function showFieldError(inputId, errorId, msg) {
      document.getElementById(inputId).classList.add('input-error');
      const errEl = document.getElementById(errorId);
      errEl.textContent = msg;
      errEl.style.display = 'block';
    }

    function clearFieldError(inputId, errorId) {
      document.getElementById(inputId).classList.remove('input-error');
      document.getElementById(errorId).style.display = 'none';
    }

    function clearAllErrors() {
      clearFieldError('currentPw', 'errorCurrent');
      clearFieldError('newPw', 'errorNew');
      clearFieldError('confirmPw', 'errorConfirm');
    }

    // Clear errors on input
    document.getElementById('currentPw').addEventListener('input', () => clearFieldError('currentPw', 'errorCurrent'));
    document.getElementById('confirmPw').addEventListener('input', () => clearFieldError('confirmPw', 'errorConfirm'));

    // ===== Toast notification =====
    function showToast(msg, isError) {
      let toast = document.getElementById('toast');
      if (!toast) {
        toast = document.createElement('div');
        toast.id = 'toast';
        toast.style.cssText = 'position:fixed; bottom:80px; left:50%; transform:translateX(-50%); padding:14px 28px; border-radius:12px; font-size:14px; z-index:9999; opacity:0; transition:opacity 0.3s; pointer-events:none; text-align:center; max-width:85%; font-weight:500;';
        document.body.appendChild(toast);
      }
      toast.textContent = msg;
      toast.style.background = isError ? '#ef4444' : '#16a34a';
      toast.style.color = 'white';
      toast.style.opacity = '1';
      setTimeout(() => { toast.style.opacity = '0'; }, 3000);
    }

    // ===== Verify current password =====
    async function verifyCurrentPassword(password) {
      // Try Supabase first
      if (SupabaseMode._ready && user.id && !user.id.startsWith('demo-')) {
        try {
          const { data, error } = await SupabaseMode.client
            .from('employees')
            .select('id, password_hash')
            .eq('id', user.id)
            .single();
          if (!error && data) {
            const storedHash = data.password_hash;
            if (storedHash && storedHash.includes(':')) {
              // 해시 비밀번호 — 서버 검증
              const res = await fetch('/api/auth', {
                method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'verify', password, storedHash })
              });
              const result = await res.json();
              return result.match === true;
            } else {
              return password === storedHash;
            }
          }
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('[PW] Supabase verify error:', e);
        }
      }

      // Fallback: demo/localStorage
      if (user.id === 'demo-admin' || user.id === 'demo-staff') {
        const storedPw = localStorage.getItem('sop_pw_' + user.email);
        return password === (storedPw || '1234');
      }
      const storedPw = localStorage.getItem('sop_pw_' + user.email);
      if (storedPw) return password === storedPw;
      return password === '1234';
    }

    // ===== Update password =====
    async function updatePassword(newPassword) {
      // Update in localStorage
      localStorage.setItem('sop_pw_' + user.email, newPassword);

      // Update in Supabase (해시 처리)
      if (SupabaseMode._ready && user.id && !user.id.startsWith('demo-')) {
        try {
          let pwHash = newPassword;
          try {
            const hashRes = await fetch('/api/auth', {
              method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
              body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'hash', password: newPassword })
            });
            const hashData = await hashRes.json();
            if (hashData.hash) pwHash = hashData.hash;
          } catch(e) { console.warn('Hash failed:', e); }

          const { error } = await SupabaseMode.client
            .from('employees')
            .update({ password_hash: pwHash })
            .eq('id', user.id);
          if (error) {
            console.error('[PW] Supabase update error:', error);
            throw error;
          }
          console.log('[PW] Supabase password updated');
        } catch (e) {
          console.error('[PW] Supabase update failed:', e);
          // localStorage was already updated, so partial success
        }
      }
    }

    // ===== Form submission =====
    document.getElementById('pwForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      clearAllErrors();

      const currentPw = document.getElementById('currentPw').value;
      const newPw = document.getElementById('newPw').value;
      const confirmPw = document.getElementById('confirmPw').value;
      const btn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');

      // Validate current password field
      if (!currentPw) {
        showFieldError('currentPw', 'errorCurrent', T('errCurrentRequired'));
        return;
      }

      // Validate new password field
      if (!newPw) {
        showFieldError('newPw', 'errorNew', T('errNewRequired'));
        return;
      }
      if (newPw.length < 4) {
        showFieldError('newPw', 'errorNew', T('errNewMin'));
        return;
      }
      if (newPw === currentPw) {
        showFieldError('newPw', 'errorNew', T('errNewSame'));
        return;
      }

      // Validate confirm password
      if (!confirmPw) {
        showFieldError('confirmPw', 'errorConfirm', T('errConfirmRequired'));
        return;
      }
      if (newPw !== confirmPw) {
        showFieldError('confirmPw', 'errorConfirm', T('errConfirmMismatch'));
        return;
      }

      // Show loading
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.textContent = T('processing');

      try {
        // Initialize Supabase if not done
        if (!SupabaseMode._ready && SupabaseMode.isEnabled()) {
          await SupabaseMode.init();
        }

        // Verify current password
        const isValid = await verifyCurrentPassword(currentPw);
        if (!isValid) {
          showFieldError('currentPw', 'errorCurrent', T('errCurrentWrong'));
          return;
        }

        // Update password
        await updatePassword(newPw);

        // Success
        showToast(T('successMsg'), false);

        // Clear form
        document.getElementById('pwForm').reset();
        document.querySelectorAll('.pw-strength-bar').forEach(bar => {
          bar.style.background = 'var(--gray-100)';
        });
        document.getElementById('strengthText').textContent = '';

        // Redirect after delay
        setTimeout(() => {
          window.location.href = 'app.html';
        }, 2000);

      } catch (err) {
        console.error('[PW] Error:', err);
        showToast(T('errorNetwork'), true);
      } finally {
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.textContent = T('submit');
      }
    });

    // ===== Init Supabase =====
    SupabaseMode.init();
  </script>

</body>
</html>


================================================================

  <script>
    // ===== 세션 타임아웃 체크 (24시간) =====
    const SESSION_HOURS = 24;
    const loginTime = localStorage.getItem('sop_login_time');
    if (loginTime && (Date.now() - parseInt(loginTime)) > SESSION_HOURS * 60 * 60 * 1000) {
      localStorage.removeItem('sop_user');
      localStorage.removeItem('sop_login_time');
    }

    // Supabase 초기화
    SupabaseMode.init().then(connected => {
      if (connected) {
        console.log('[Login] Supabase 모드 활성화');
      }
    });

    // ===== 다국어 텍스트 =====
    const TEXTS = {

    let currentLang = localStorage.getItem('sop_lang') || CONFIG.DEFAULT_LANG;

    function setLang(lang) {
      currentLang = lang;
      localStorage.setItem('sop_lang', lang);
      updateTexts();
    }

    function updateTexts() {
      const t = TEXTS[currentLang];
      document.querySelector('.login-card h1').textContent = t.title;
      document.querySelector('.login-card .subtitle').textContent = t.subtitle;
      document.querySelector('label[for="email"]').textContent = t.email;
      document.querySelector('label[for="password"]').textContent = t.password;
      document.getElementById('email').placeholder = t.emailPlaceholder;
      document.getElementById('password').placeholder = t.passwordPlaceholder;
      document.getElementById('loginBtn').textContent = t.login;
      document.getElementById('forgotLink').textContent = t.forgotPassword;
      document.getElementById('resetTitle').textContent = t.resetTitle;
      document.getElementById('resetDesc').textContent = t.resetDesc;
      document.getElementById('resetEmail').placeholder = t.resetPlaceholder;
    }

    // 페이지 로드시 언어 적용
    updateTexts();

    // ===== 비밀번호 재설정 =====
    function showPasswordReset() {
      const form = document.getElementById('resetForm');
      form.style.display = form.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
    }

    async function handlePasswordReset() {
      const email = document.getElementById('resetEmail').value.trim();
      const result = document.getElementById('resetResult');
      const tx = TEXTS[currentLang];
      if (!email) { result.textContent = tx.resetEnterEmail; result.style.color = 'var(--danger)'; result.style.display = 'block'; return; }

      // Supabase에서 확인 후 임시 비밀번호 설정
      if (window.SupabaseMode && SupabaseMode._ready) {
        try {
          const { data, error } = await SupabaseMode.client
            .from('employees')
            .select('id, name')
            .eq('email', email)
            .single();

          if (data) {
            const tempPw = Math.random().toString(36).slice(-6);
            await SupabaseMode.client
              .from('employees')
              .update({ password_hash: tempPw })
              .eq('email', email);

            result.innerHTML = `✅ ${tx.resetTempPw}: <strong style="font-size:18px;color:var(--primary);">${tempPw}</strong><br><span style="font-size:12px;">${tx.resetTempPwSub}</span>`;
            result.style.color = 'var(--success)';
            result.style.display = 'block';
            return;
          }
        } catch(e) { console.error('Reset error:', e); }
      }

      // 데모 계정 체크 (폴백)
      const demoAccounts = {'admin@test.com': tx.admin, 'manager@test.com': '지점장', 'staff@test.com': tx.staff};
      if (demoAccounts[email]) {
        result.innerHTML = `✅ <strong>${demoAccounts[email]}</strong> ${tx.resetAccountIs}<br>${tx.password}: <strong style="font-size:18px;color:var(--primary);">1234</strong>`;
        result.style.color = 'var(--success)';
      } else {
        result.textContent = tx.resetNotFound;
        result.style.color = 'var(--danger)';
      }
      result.style.display = 'block';
    }

    // ===== 로그인 처리 =====
    document.getElementById('loginForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();

      const email = document.getElementById('email').value.trim();
      const password = document.getElementById('password').value;
      const btn = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
      const errorDiv = document.getElementById('errorMsg');

      // 버튼 로딩 상태
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner"></span>';
      errorDiv.style.display = 'none';

      try {
        let user = null;

        // Supabase 모드: DB에서 직원 조회
        if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
          user = await SupabaseMode.login(email, password);
        }

        // Supabase에서 못 찾으면 데모 로그인 시도
        if (!user) {
          if (email === 'admin@test.com' && password === '1234') {
            user = { id: 'demo-admin', email, role: 'admin', name: '관리자', adminRole: 'superadmin' };
          } else if (email === 'manager@test.com' && password === '1234') {
            user = { id: 'demo-manager', email, role: 'admin', name: '강남점장', adminRole: 'branch_manager', adminBranch: '서울 강남점' };
          } else if (email === 'staff@test.com' && password === '1234') {
            user = { id: 'demo-staff', email, role: 'staff', name: '직원1' };
          }
        }

        if (!user) throw new Error('invalid');

        // 로그인 성공 → 세션 저장
        localStorage.setItem('sop_user', JSON.stringify(user));
        localStorage.setItem('sop_login_time', Date.now().toString());

        // Supabase에서 데이터 동기화
        if (SupabaseMode._ready) {
          await SupabaseMode.syncAll();
        }

        // 역할별 페이지 이동
        if (user.role === 'admin') {
          window.location.href = 'admin/index.html';
        } else {
          window.location.href = 'app.html';
        }

      } catch (err) {
        const t = TEXTS[currentLang];
        errorDiv.textContent = err.message === 'invalid'
          ? t.errorInvalid
          : t.errorNetwork;
        errorDiv.style.display = 'block';
      } finally {
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.textContent = TEXTS[currentLang].login;
      }
    });
  </script>

</body>
</html>
